3343 //------------------------------as_klass_type----------------------------------
3344 // Return the klass type corresponding to this instance or array type.
3345 // It is the type that is loaded from an object of this type.
3346 const TypeKlassPtr* TypeOopPtr::as_klass_type() const {
3347   ciKlass* k = klass();
3348   bool    xk = klass_is_exact();
3349   if (k == NULL)
3350     return TypeKlassPtr::OBJECT;
3351   else
3352     return TypeKlassPtr::make(xk? Constant: NotNull, k, Offset(0), isa_instptr() && is_instptr()->flat_array());
3353 }
3354 
3355 //------------------------------meet-------------------------------------------
3356 // Compute the MEET of two types.  It returns a new Type object.
3357 const Type *TypeOopPtr::xmeet_helper(const Type *t) const {
3358   // Perform a fast test for common case; meeting the same types together.
3359   if( this == t ) return this;  // Meeting same type-rep?
3360 
3361   // Current "this->_base" is OopPtr
3362   switch (t->base()) {          // switch on original type
3363 
3364   case Int:                     // Mixing ints & oops happens when javac
3365   case Long:                    // reuses local variables
3366   case FloatTop:
3367   case FloatCon:
3368   case FloatBot:
3369   case DoubleTop:
3370   case DoubleCon:
3371   case DoubleBot:
3372   case NarrowOop:
3373   case NarrowKlass:
3374   case Bottom:                  // Ye Olde Default
3375     return Type::BOTTOM;
3376   case Top:
3377     return this;
3378 
3379   default:                      // All else is a mistake
3380     typerr(t);
3381 
3382   case RawPtr:
3383   case MetadataPtr:
3384   case KlassPtr:
3385     return TypePtr::BOTTOM;     // Oop meet raw is not well defined
3386 
3387   case AnyPtr: {
3388     // Found an AnyPtr type vs self-OopPtr type
3389     const TypePtr *tp = t->is_ptr();
3390     Offset offset = meet_offset(tp->offset());
3391     PTR ptr = meet_ptr(tp->ptr());
3392     const TypePtr* speculative = xmeet_speculative(tp);
3393     int depth = meet_inline_depth(tp->inline_depth());
3394     switch (tp->ptr()) {
3395     case Null:
3396       if (ptr == Null)  return TypePtr::make(AnyPtr, ptr, offset, speculative, depth);
3397       // else fall through:
3398     case TopPTR:
3399     case AnyNull: {
3400       int instance_id = meet_instance_id(InstanceTop);
3401       return make(ptr, offset, instance_id, speculative, depth);
3402     }
3403     case BotPTR:
3404     case NotNull:
3405       return TypePtr::make(AnyPtr, ptr, offset, speculative, depth);
3406     default: typerr(t);
3407     }
3408   }
3409 
3410   case OopPtr: {                 // Meeting to other OopPtrs

3412     int instance_id = meet_instance_id(tp->instance_id());
3413     const TypePtr* speculative = xmeet_speculative(tp);
3414     int depth = meet_inline_depth(tp->inline_depth());
3415     return make(meet_ptr(tp->ptr()), meet_offset(tp->offset()), instance_id, speculative, depth);
3416   }
3417 
3418   case InstPtr:                  // For these, flip the call around to cut down
3419   case AryPtr:
3420     return t->xmeet(this);      // Call in reverse direction
3421 
3422   } // End of switch
3423   return this;                  // Return the double constant
3424 }
3425 
3426 
3427 //------------------------------xdual------------------------------------------
3428 // Dual of a pure heap pointer.  No relevant klass or oop information.
3429 const Type *TypeOopPtr::xdual() const {
3430   assert(klass() == Compile::current()->env()->Object_klass(), "no klasses here");
3431   assert(const_oop() == NULL,             "no constants here");
3432   return new TypeOopPtr(_base, dual_ptr(), klass(), klass_is_exact(), const_oop(), dual_offset(), Offset::bottom, dual_instance_id(), dual_speculative(), dual_inline_depth());
3433 }
3434 
3435 //--------------------------make_from_klass_common-----------------------------
3436 // Computes the element-type given a klass.
3437 const TypeOopPtr* TypeOopPtr::make_from_klass_common(ciKlass *klass, bool klass_change, bool try_for_exact) {
3438   if (klass->is_instance_klass() || klass->is_inlinetype()) {
3439     Compile* C = Compile::current();
3440     Dependencies* deps = C->dependencies();
3441     assert((deps != NULL) == (C->method() != NULL && C->method()->code_size() > 0), "sanity");
3442     // Element is an instance
3443     bool klass_is_exact = false;
3444     if (klass->is_loaded()) {
3445       // Try to set klass_is_exact.
3446       ciInstanceKlass* ik = klass->as_instance_klass();
3447       klass_is_exact = ik->is_final();
3448       if (!klass_is_exact && klass_change
3449           && deps != NULL && UseUniqueSubclasses) {
3450         ciInstanceKlass* sub = ik->unique_concrete_subklass();
3451         if (sub != NULL) {
3452           deps->assert_abstract_with_unique_concrete_subtype(ik, sub);
3453           klass = ik = sub;
3454           klass_is_exact = sub->is_final();
3455         }
3456       }
3457       if (!klass_is_exact && try_for_exact && deps != NULL &&
3458           !ik->is_interface() && !ik->has_subklass()) {
3459         // Add a dependence; if concrete subclass added we need to recompile
3460         deps->assert_leaf_type(ik);
3461         klass_is_exact = true;
3462       }
3463     }
3464     return TypeInstPtr::make(TypePtr::BotPTR, klass, klass_is_exact, NULL, Offset(0), klass->flatten_array());
3465   } else if (klass->is_obj_array_klass()) {
3466     // Element is an object or inline type array. Recursively call ourself.
3467     const TypeOopPtr* etype = TypeOopPtr::make_from_klass_common(klass->as_array_klass()->element_klass(), /* klass_change= */ false, try_for_exact);
3468     if (etype->is_inlinetypeptr()) {
3469       etype = etype->join_speculative(TypePtr::NOTNULL)->is_oopptr();
3470     }
3471     // Determine null-free/flattened properties
3472     const TypeOopPtr* exact_etype = etype;
3473     if (etype->can_be_inline_type()) {
3474       // Use exact type if element can be an inline type
3475       exact_etype = TypeOopPtr::make_from_klass_common(klass->as_array_klass()->element_klass(), /* klass_change= */ true, /* try_for_exact= */ true);
3476     }
3477     bool not_null_free = !exact_etype->can_be_inline_type();
3478     bool not_flat = !UseFlatArray || not_null_free || (exact_etype->is_inlinetypeptr() && !exact_etype->inline_klass()->flatten_array());
3479 
3480     bool xk = etype->klass_is_exact();
3481     const TypeAry* arr0 = TypeAry::make(etype, TypeInt::POS, false, not_flat, not_null_free);
3482     // We used to pass NotNull in here, asserting that the sub-arrays
3483     // are all not-null.  This is not true in generally, as code can
3484     // slam NULLs down in the subarrays.
3485     const TypeAryPtr* arr = TypeAryPtr::make(TypePtr::BotPTR, arr0, klass, xk, Offset(0));
3486     return arr;
3487   } else if (klass->is_type_array_klass()) {
3488     // Element is an typeArray
3489     const Type* etype = get_const_basic_type(klass->as_type_array_klass()->element_type());
3490     const TypeAry* arr0 = TypeAry::make(etype, TypeInt::POS,
3491                                         /* stable= */ false, /* not_flat= */ true, /* not_null_free= */ true);
3492     // We used to pass NotNull in here, asserting that the array pointer
3493     // is not-null. That was not true in general.
3494     const TypeAryPtr* arr = TypeAryPtr::make(TypePtr::BotPTR, arr0, klass, true, Offset(0));
3495     return arr;
3496   } else if (klass->is_flat_array_klass()) {
3497     ciInlineKlass* vk = klass->as_array_klass()->element_klass()->as_inline_klass();
3498     const TypeAry* arr0 = TypeAry::make(TypeInlineType::make(vk), TypeInt::POS);
3499     const TypeAryPtr* arr = TypeAryPtr::make(TypePtr::BotPTR, arr0, klass, true, Offset(0));
3500     return arr;
3501   } else {
3502     ShouldNotReachHere();
3503     return NULL;
3504   }
3505 }
3506 
3507 //------------------------------make_from_constant-----------------------------
3508 // Make a java pointer from an oop constant
3509 const TypeOopPtr* TypeOopPtr::make_from_constant(ciObject* o, bool require_constant) {
3510   assert(!o->is_null_object(), "null object not yet handled here.");
3511 
3512   const bool make_constant = require_constant || o->should_be_constant();
3513 
3514   ciKlass* klass = o->klass();
3515   if (klass->is_instance_klass() || klass->is_inlinetype()) {
3516     // Element is an instance or inline type
3517     if (make_constant) {
3518       return TypeInstPtr::make(o);
3519     } else {
3520       return TypeInstPtr::make(TypePtr::NotNull, klass, true, NULL, Offset(0), klass->flatten_array());
3521     }
3522   } else if (klass->is_obj_array_klass()) {
3523     // Element is an object array. Recursively call ourself.
3524     const TypeOopPtr* etype = TypeOopPtr::make_from_klass_raw(klass->as_array_klass()->element_klass());
3525     bool null_free = false;
3526     if (etype->is_inlinetypeptr()) {
3527       null_free = true;
3528       etype = etype->join_speculative(TypePtr::NOTNULL)->is_oopptr();
3529     }
3530     const TypeAry* arr0 = TypeAry::make(etype, TypeInt::make(o->as_array()->length()),
3531                                         /* stable= */ false, /* not_flat= */ true, /* not_null_free= */ !null_free);
3532     // We used to pass NotNull in here, asserting that the sub-arrays
3533     // are all not-null.  This is not true in generally, as code can
3534     // slam NULLs down in the subarrays.
3535     if (make_constant) {
3536       return TypeAryPtr::make(TypePtr::Constant, o, arr0, klass, true, Offset(0));
3537     } else {
3538       return TypeAryPtr::make(TypePtr::NotNull, arr0, klass, true, Offset(0));
3539     }
3540   } else if (klass->is_type_array_klass()) {
3541     // Element is an typeArray
3542     const Type* etype = (Type*)get_const_basic_type(klass->as_type_array_klass()->element_type());
3543     const TypeAry* arr0 = TypeAry::make(etype, TypeInt::make(o->as_array()->length()),
3544                                         /* stable= */ false, /* not_flat= */ true, /* not_null_free= */ true);
3545     // We used to pass NotNull in here, asserting that the array pointer
3546     // is not-null. That was not true in general.
3547     if (make_constant) {
3548       return TypeAryPtr::make(TypePtr::Constant, o, arr0, klass, true, Offset(0));
3549     } else {
3550       return TypeAryPtr::make(TypePtr::NotNull, arr0, klass, true, Offset(0));
3551     }
3552   } else if (klass->is_flat_array_klass()) {
3553     ciInlineKlass* vk = klass->as_array_klass()->element_klass()->as_inline_klass();
3554     const TypeAry* arr0 = TypeAry::make(TypeInlineType::make(vk), TypeInt::make(o->as_array()->length()));
3555     // We used to pass NotNull in here, asserting that the sub-arrays
3556     // are all not-null.  This is not true in generally, as code can
3557     // slam NULLs down in the subarrays.
3558     if (make_constant) {
3559       return TypeAryPtr::make(TypePtr::Constant, o, arr0, klass, true, Offset(0));
3560     } else {
3561       return TypeAryPtr::make(TypePtr::NotNull, arr0, klass, true, Offset(0));
3562     }
3563   }
3564 
3565   fatal("unhandled object type");
3566   return NULL;
3567 }
3568 
3569 //------------------------------get_con----------------------------------------
3570 intptr_t TypeOopPtr::get_con() const {
3571   assert( _ptr == Null || _ptr == Constant, "" );
3572   assert(offset() >= 0, "");
3573 
3574   if (offset() != 0) {
3575     // After being ported to the compiler interface, the compiler no longer
3576     // directly manipulates the addresses of oops.  Rather, it only has a pointer
3577     // to a handle at compile time.  This handle is embedded in the generated
3578     // code and dereferenced at the time the nmethod is made.  Until that time,
3579     // it is not reasonable to do arithmetic with the addresses of oops (we don't
3580     // have access to the addresses!).  This does not seem to currently happen,
3581     // but this assertion here is to help prevent its occurence.
3582     tty->print_cr("Found oop constant with non-zero offset");
3583     ShouldNotReachHere();
3584   }
3585 
3586   return (intptr_t)const_oop()->constant_encoding();
3587 }

3591 // Do not allow interface-vs.-noninterface joins to collapse to top.
3592 const Type *TypeOopPtr::filter_helper(const Type *kills, bool include_speculative) const {
3593 
3594   const Type* ft = join_helper(kills, include_speculative);

3647     return (one == two) && TypePtr::eq(t);
3648   } else {
3649     return one->equals(two) && TypePtr::eq(t);
3650   }
3651 }

3653 //------------------------------hash-------------------------------------------
3654 // Type-specific hashing function.
3655 int TypeOopPtr::hash(void) const {
3656   return
3657     java_add(java_add((jint)(const_oop() ? const_oop()->hash() : 0), (jint)_klass_is_exact),
3658              java_add((jint)_instance_id, (jint)TypePtr::hash()));
3659 }

3661 //------------------------------dump2------------------------------------------
3662 #ifndef PRODUCT
3663 void TypeOopPtr::dump2( Dict &d, uint depth, outputStream *st ) const {
3664   st->print("oopptr:%s", ptr_msg[_ptr]);
3665   if( _klass_is_exact ) st->print(":exact");
3666   if( const_oop() ) st->print(INTPTR_FORMAT, p2i(const_oop()));
3667   _offset.dump2(st);





3668   if (_instance_id == InstanceTop)
3669     st->print(",iid=top");
3670   else if (_instance_id != InstanceBot)
3671     st->print(",iid=%d",_instance_id);
3672 
3673   dump_inline_depth(st);
3674   dump_speculative(st);
3675 }
3676 #endif

3678 //------------------------------singleton--------------------------------------
3679 // TRUE if Type is a singleton type, FALSE otherwise.   Singletons are simple
3680 // constants
3681 bool TypeOopPtr::singleton(void) const {
3682   // detune optimizer to not generate constant oop + constant offset as a constant!
3683   // TopPTR, Null, AnyNull, Constant are all singletons
3684   return (offset() == 0) && !below_centerline(_ptr);
3685 }
3686 
3687 //------------------------------add_offset-------------------------------------
3688 const TypePtr *TypeOopPtr::add_offset(intptr_t offset) const {
3689   return make(_ptr, xadd_offset(offset), _instance_id, add_offset_speculative(offset), _inline_depth);
3690 }
3691 
3692 /**
3693  * Return same type without a speculative part
3694  */
3695 const Type* TypeOopPtr::remove_speculative() const {
3696   if (_speculative == NULL) {
3697     return this;
3698   }
3699   assert(_inline_depth == InlineDepthTop || _inline_depth == InlineDepthBottom, "non speculative type shouldn't have inline depth");
3700   return make(_ptr, _offset, _instance_id, NULL, _inline_depth);
3701 }
3702 
3703 /**
3704  * Return same type but drop speculative part if we know we won't use

3756  *
3757  * @return  true if type profile is valuable
3758  */
3759 bool TypeOopPtr::would_improve_type(ciKlass* exact_kls, int inline_depth) const {
3760   // no way to improve an already exact type
3761   if (klass_is_exact()) {
3762     return false;
3763   }
3764   return TypePtr::would_improve_type(exact_kls, inline_depth);
3765 }

3767 //=============================================================================
3768 // Convenience common pre-built types.
3769 const TypeInstPtr *TypeInstPtr::NOTNULL;
3770 const TypeInstPtr *TypeInstPtr::BOTTOM;
3771 const TypeInstPtr *TypeInstPtr::MIRROR;
3772 const TypeInstPtr *TypeInstPtr::MARK;
3773 const TypeInstPtr *TypeInstPtr::KLASS;
3774 
3775 //------------------------------TypeInstPtr-------------------------------------
3776 TypeInstPtr::TypeInstPtr(PTR ptr, ciKlass* k, bool xk, ciObject* o, Offset off,
3777                          bool flat_array, int instance_id, const TypePtr* speculative,
3778                          int inline_depth)
3779   : TypeOopPtr(InstPtr, ptr, k, xk, o, off, Offset::bottom, instance_id, speculative, inline_depth),
3780     _name(k->name()), _flat_array(flat_array) {
3781    assert(k != NULL &&
3782           (k->is_loaded() || o == NULL),
3783           "cannot have constants with non-loaded klass");
3784    assert(!klass()->is_inlinetype() || !klass()->flatten_array() || flat_array, "incorrect flatten array bit");
3785    assert(!flat_array || can_be_inline_type(), "incorrect flatten array bit");
3786 };
3787 
3788 //------------------------------make-------------------------------------------
3789 const TypeInstPtr *TypeInstPtr::make(PTR ptr,
3790                                      ciKlass* k,
3791                                      bool xk,
3792                                      ciObject* o,
3793                                      Offset offset,
3794                                      bool flat_array,
3795                                      int instance_id,
3796                                      const TypePtr* speculative,
3797                                      int inline_depth) {
3798   assert( !k->is_loaded() || k->is_instance_klass(), "Must be for instance");
3799   // Either const_oop() is NULL or else ptr is Constant
3800   assert( (!o && ptr != Constant) || (o && ptr == Constant),
3801           "constant pointers must have a value supplied" );
3802   // Ptr is never Null
3803   assert( ptr != Null, "NULL pointers are not typed" );
3804 
3805   assert(instance_id <= 0 || xk, "instances are always exactly typed");
3806   if (ptr == Constant) {
3807     // Note:  This case includes meta-object constants, such as methods.
3808     xk = true;
3809   } else if (k->is_loaded()) {
3810     ciInstanceKlass* ik = k->as_instance_klass();
3811     if (!xk && ik->is_final())     xk = true;   // no inexact final klass
3812     if (xk && ik->is_interface())  xk = false;  // no exact interface
3813   }
3814 
3815   // Now hash this baby
3816   TypeInstPtr *result =
3817     (TypeInstPtr*)(new TypeInstPtr(ptr, k, xk, o ,offset, flat_array, instance_id, speculative, inline_depth))->hashcons();
3818 
3819   return result;
3820 }
3821 
3822 /**
3823  *  Create constant type for a constant boxed value
3824  */
3825 const Type* TypeInstPtr::get_const_boxed_value() const {
3826   assert(is_ptr_to_boxed_value(), "should be called only for boxed value");
3827   assert((const_oop() != NULL), "should be called only for constant object");
3828   ciConstant constant = const_oop()->as_instance()->field_value_by_offset(offset());
3829   BasicType bt = constant.basic_type();
3830   switch (bt) {
3831     case T_BOOLEAN:  return TypeInt::make(constant.as_boolean());
3832     case T_INT:      return TypeInt::make(constant.as_int());
3833     case T_CHAR:     return TypeInt::make(constant.as_char());
3834     case T_BYTE:     return TypeInt::make(constant.as_byte());
3835     case T_SHORT:    return TypeInt::make(constant.as_short());
3836     case T_FLOAT:    return TypeF::make(constant.as_float());
3837     case T_DOUBLE:   return TypeD::make(constant.as_double());
3838     case T_LONG:     return TypeLong::make(constant.as_long());
3839     default:         break;
3840   }
3841   fatal("Invalid boxed value type '%s'", type2name(bt));
3842   return NULL;
3843 }
3844 
3845 //------------------------------cast_to_ptr_type-------------------------------
3846 const Type *TypeInstPtr::cast_to_ptr_type(PTR ptr) const {
3847   if( ptr == _ptr ) return this;
3848   // Reconstruct _sig info here since not a problem with later lazy
3849   // construction, _sig will show up on demand.
3850   return make(ptr, klass(), klass_is_exact(), const_oop(), _offset, _flat_array, _instance_id, _speculative, _inline_depth);
3851 }
3852 
3853 
3854 //-----------------------------cast_to_exactness-------------------------------
3855 const Type *TypeInstPtr::cast_to_exactness(bool klass_is_exact) const {
3856   if( klass_is_exact == _klass_is_exact ) return this;
3857   if (!_klass->is_loaded())  return this;
3858   ciInstanceKlass* ik = _klass->as_instance_klass();
3859   if( (ik->is_final() || _const_oop) )  return this;  // cannot clear xk
3860   if( ik->is_interface() )              return this;  // cannot set xk
3861   return make(ptr(), klass(), klass_is_exact, const_oop(), _offset, _flat_array, _instance_id, _speculative, _inline_depth);
3862 }
3863 
3864 //-----------------------------cast_to_instance_id----------------------------
3865 const TypeOopPtr *TypeInstPtr::cast_to_instance_id(int instance_id) const {
3866   if( instance_id == _instance_id ) return this;
3867   return make(_ptr, klass(), _klass_is_exact, const_oop(), _offset, _flat_array, instance_id, _speculative, _inline_depth);
3868 }
3869 
3870 //------------------------------xmeet_unloaded---------------------------------
3871 // Compute the MEET of two InstPtrs when at least one is unloaded.
3872 // Assume classes are different since called after check for same name/class-loader
3873 const TypeInstPtr *TypeInstPtr::xmeet_unloaded(const TypeInstPtr *tinst) const {
3874     Offset off = meet_offset(tinst->offset());
3875     PTR ptr = meet_ptr(tinst->ptr());
3876     int instance_id = meet_instance_id(tinst->instance_id());
3877     const TypePtr* speculative = xmeet_speculative(tinst);
3878     int depth = meet_inline_depth(tinst->inline_depth());
3879 
3880     const TypeInstPtr *loaded    = is_loaded() ? this  : tinst;
3881     const TypeInstPtr *unloaded  = is_loaded() ? tinst : this;
3882     if( loaded->klass()->equals(ciEnv::current()->Object_klass()) ) {
3883       //
3884       // Meet unloaded class with java/lang/Object
3885       //
3886       // Meet
3887       //          |                     Unloaded Class
3888       //  Object  |   TOP    |   AnyNull | Constant |   NotNull |  BOTTOM   |
3889       //  ===================================================================
3890       //   TOP    | ..........................Unloaded......................|
3891       //  AnyNull |  U-AN    |................Unloaded......................|
3892       // Constant | ... O-NN .................................. |   O-BOT   |
3893       //  NotNull | ... O-NN .................................. |   O-BOT   |
3894       //  BOTTOM  | ........................Object-BOTTOM ..................|
3895       //
3896       assert(loaded->ptr() != TypePtr::Null, "insanity check");
3897       //
3898       if(      loaded->ptr() == TypePtr::TopPTR ) { return unloaded; }
3899       else if (loaded->ptr() == TypePtr::AnyNull) { return TypeInstPtr::make(ptr, unloaded->klass(), false, NULL, off, false, instance_id, speculative, depth); }
3900       else if (loaded->ptr() == TypePtr::BotPTR ) { return TypeInstPtr::BOTTOM; }
3901       else if (loaded->ptr() == TypePtr::Constant || loaded->ptr() == TypePtr::NotNull) {
3902         if (unloaded->ptr() == TypePtr::BotPTR  ) { return TypeInstPtr::BOTTOM;  }
3903         else                                      { return TypeInstPtr::NOTNULL; }
3904       }
3905       else if( unloaded->ptr() == TypePtr::TopPTR )  { return unloaded; }
3906 
3907       return unloaded->cast_to_ptr_type(TypePtr::AnyNull)->is_instptr();
3908     }
3909 
3910     // Both are unloaded, not the same class, not Object
3911     // Or meet unloaded with a different loaded class, not java/lang/Object
3912     if( ptr != TypePtr::BotPTR ) {
3913       return TypeInstPtr::NOTNULL;
3914     }
3915     return TypeInstPtr::BOTTOM;
3916 }
3917 
3918 
3919 //------------------------------meet-------------------------------------------

3932   case FloatBot:
3933   case DoubleTop:
3934   case DoubleCon:
3935   case DoubleBot:
3936   case NarrowOop:
3937   case NarrowKlass:
3938   case Bottom:                  // Ye Olde Default
3939     return Type::BOTTOM;
3940   case Top:
3941     return this;
3942 
3943   default:                      // All else is a mistake
3944     typerr(t);
3945 
3946   case MetadataPtr:
3947   case KlassPtr:
3948   case RawPtr: return TypePtr::BOTTOM;
3949 
3950   case AryPtr: {                // All arrays inherit from Object class
3951     const TypeAryPtr *tp = t->is_aryptr();
3952     Offset offset = meet_offset(tp->offset());
3953     PTR ptr = meet_ptr(tp->ptr());
3954     int instance_id = meet_instance_id(tp->instance_id());
3955     const TypePtr* speculative = xmeet_speculative(tp);
3956     int depth = meet_inline_depth(tp->inline_depth());
3957     switch (ptr) {
3958     case TopPTR:
3959     case AnyNull:                // Fall 'down' to dual of object klass
3960       // For instances when a subclass meets a superclass we fall
3961       // below the centerline when the superclass is exact. We need to
3962       // do the same here.
3963       if (klass()->equals(ciEnv::current()->Object_klass()) && !klass_is_exact() && !flat_array()) {
3964         return TypeAryPtr::make(ptr, tp->ary(), tp->klass(), tp->klass_is_exact(), offset, tp->field_offset(), instance_id, speculative, depth);
3965       } else {
3966         // cannot subclass, so the meet has to fall badly below the centerline
3967         ptr = NotNull;
3968         instance_id = InstanceBot;
3969         return TypeInstPtr::make( ptr, ciEnv::current()->Object_klass(), false, NULL, offset, false, instance_id, speculative, depth);
3970       }
3971     case Constant:
3972     case NotNull:
3973     case BotPTR:                // Fall down to object klass
3974       // LCA is object_klass, but if we subclass from the top we can do better
3975       if( above_centerline(_ptr) ) { // if( _ptr == TopPTR || _ptr == AnyNull )
3976         // If 'this' (InstPtr) is above the centerline and it is Object class
3977         // then we can subclass in the Java class hierarchy.
3978         // For instances when a subclass meets a superclass we fall
3979         // below the centerline when the superclass is exact. We need
3980         // to do the same here.
3981         if (klass()->equals(ciEnv::current()->Object_klass()) && !klass_is_exact() && !flat_array()) {
3982           // that is, tp's array type is a subtype of my klass
3983           return TypeAryPtr::make(ptr, (ptr == Constant ? tp->const_oop() : NULL),
3984                                   tp->ary(), tp->klass(), tp->klass_is_exact(), offset, tp->field_offset(), instance_id, speculative, depth);
3985         }
3986       }
3987       // The other case cannot happen, since I cannot be a subtype of an array.
3988       // The meet falls down to Object class below centerline.
3989       if( ptr == Constant )
3990          ptr = NotNull;
3991       instance_id = InstanceBot;
3992       return make(ptr, ciEnv::current()->Object_klass(), false, NULL, offset, false, instance_id, speculative, depth);
3993     default: typerr(t);
3994     }
3995   }
3996 
3997   case OopPtr: {                // Meeting to OopPtrs
3998     // Found a OopPtr type vs self-InstPtr type
3999     const TypeOopPtr *tp = t->is_oopptr();
4000     Offset offset = meet_offset(tp->offset());
4001     PTR ptr = meet_ptr(tp->ptr());
4002     switch (tp->ptr()) {
4003     case TopPTR:
4004     case AnyNull: {
4005       int instance_id = meet_instance_id(InstanceTop);
4006       const TypePtr* speculative = xmeet_speculative(tp);
4007       int depth = meet_inline_depth(tp->inline_depth());
4008       return make(ptr, klass(), klass_is_exact(),
4009                   (ptr == Constant ? const_oop() : NULL), offset, flat_array(), instance_id, speculative, depth);
4010     }
4011     case NotNull:
4012     case BotPTR: {
4013       int instance_id = meet_instance_id(tp->instance_id());
4014       const TypePtr* speculative = xmeet_speculative(tp);
4015       int depth = meet_inline_depth(tp->inline_depth());
4016       return TypeOopPtr::make(ptr, offset, instance_id, speculative, depth);
4017     }
4018     default: typerr(t);
4019     }
4020   }
4021 
4022   case AnyPtr: {                // Meeting to AnyPtrs
4023     // Found an AnyPtr type vs self-InstPtr type
4024     const TypePtr *tp = t->is_ptr();
4025     Offset offset = meet_offset(tp->offset());
4026     PTR ptr = meet_ptr(tp->ptr());
4027     int instance_id = meet_instance_id(InstanceTop);
4028     const TypePtr* speculative = xmeet_speculative(tp);
4029     int depth = meet_inline_depth(tp->inline_depth());
4030     switch (tp->ptr()) {
4031     case Null:
4032       if( ptr == Null ) return TypePtr::make(AnyPtr, ptr, offset, speculative, depth);
4033       // else fall through to AnyNull
4034     case TopPTR:
4035     case AnyNull: {
4036       return make(ptr, klass(), klass_is_exact(),
4037                   (ptr == Constant ? const_oop() : NULL), offset, flat_array(), instance_id, speculative, depth);
4038     }
4039     case NotNull:
4040     case BotPTR:
4041       return TypePtr::make(AnyPtr, ptr, offset, speculative,depth);
4042     default: typerr(t);
4043     }
4044   }
4045 
4046   /*
4047                  A-top         }
4048                /   |   \       }  Tops
4049            B-top A-any C-top   }
4050               | /  |  \ |      }  Any-nulls
4051            B-any   |   C-any   }
4052               |    |    |
4053            B-con A-con C-con   } constants; not comparable across classes
4054               |    |    |
4055            B-not   |   C-not   }
4056               | \  |  / |      }  not-nulls
4057            B-bot A-not C-bot   }
4058                \   |   /       }  Bottoms
4059                  A-bot         }
4060   */
4061 
4062   case InstPtr: {                // Meeting 2 Oops?
4063     // Found an InstPtr sub-type vs self-InstPtr type
4064     const TypeInstPtr *tinst = t->is_instptr();
4065     Offset off = meet_offset( tinst->offset() );
4066     PTR ptr = meet_ptr( tinst->ptr() );
4067     int instance_id = meet_instance_id(tinst->instance_id());
4068     const TypePtr* speculative = xmeet_speculative(tinst);
4069     int depth = meet_inline_depth(tinst->inline_depth());
4070 
4071     // Check for easy case; klasses are equal (and perhaps not loaded!)
4072     // If we have constants, then we created oops so classes are loaded
4073     // and we can handle the constants further down.  This case handles
4074     // both-not-loaded or both-loaded classes
4075     if (ptr != Constant && klass()->equals(tinst->klass()) && klass_is_exact() == tinst->klass_is_exact() &&
4076         flat_array() == tinst->flat_array()) {
4077       return make(ptr, klass(), klass_is_exact(), NULL, off, flat_array(), instance_id, speculative, depth);
4078     }
4079 
4080     // Classes require inspection in the Java klass hierarchy.  Must be loaded.
4081     ciKlass* tinst_klass = tinst->klass();
4082     ciKlass* this_klass  = this->klass();
4083     bool tinst_xk = tinst->klass_is_exact();
4084     bool this_xk  = this->klass_is_exact();
4085     bool tinst_flat_array = tinst->flat_array();
4086     bool this_flat_array  = this->flat_array();
4087     if (!tinst_klass->is_loaded() || !this_klass->is_loaded() ) {
4088       // One of these classes has not been loaded
4089       const TypeInstPtr *unloaded_meet = xmeet_unloaded(tinst);
4090 #ifndef PRODUCT
4091       if( PrintOpto && Verbose ) {
4092         tty->print("meet of unloaded classes resulted in: "); unloaded_meet->dump(); tty->cr();
4093         tty->print("  this == "); this->dump(); tty->cr();
4094         tty->print(" tinst == "); tinst->dump(); tty->cr();
4095       }
4096 #endif
4097       return unloaded_meet;
4098     }
4099 
4100     // Handle mixing oops and interfaces first.
4101     if( this_klass->is_interface() && !(tinst_klass->is_interface() ||
4102                                         tinst_klass == ciEnv::current()->Object_klass())) {
4103       ciKlass *tmp = tinst_klass; // Swap interface around
4104       tinst_klass = this_klass;
4105       this_klass = tmp;
4106       bool tmp2 = tinst_xk;
4107       tinst_xk = this_xk;
4108       this_xk = tmp2;
4109       tmp2 = tinst_flat_array;
4110       tinst_flat_array = this_flat_array;
4111       this_flat_array = tmp2;
4112     }
4113     if (tinst_klass->is_interface() &&
4114         !(this_klass->is_interface() ||
4115           // Treat java/lang/Object as an honorary interface,
4116           // because we need a bottom for the interface hierarchy.
4117           this_klass == ciEnv::current()->Object_klass())) {
4118       // Oop meets interface!
4119 
4120       // See if the oop subtypes (implements) interface.
4121       ciKlass *k;
4122       bool xk;
4123       bool flat_array;
4124       if( this_klass->is_subtype_of( tinst_klass ) ) {
4125         // Oop indeed subtypes.  Now keep oop or interface depending
4126         // on whether we are both above the centerline or either is
4127         // below the centerline.  If we are on the centerline
4128         // (e.g., Constant vs. AnyNull interface), use the constant.
4129         k  = below_centerline(ptr) ? tinst_klass : this_klass;
4130         // If we are keeping this_klass, keep its exactness too.
4131         xk = below_centerline(ptr) ? tinst_xk    : this_xk;
4132         flat_array = below_centerline(ptr) ? tinst_flat_array    : this_flat_array;
4133       } else {                  // Does not implement, fall to Object
4134         // Oop does not implement interface, so mixing falls to Object
4135         // just like the verifier does (if both are above the
4136         // centerline fall to interface)
4137         k = above_centerline(ptr) ? tinst_klass : ciEnv::current()->Object_klass();
4138         xk = above_centerline(ptr) ? tinst_xk : false;
4139         flat_array = above_centerline(ptr) ? tinst_flat_array : false;
4140         // Watch out for Constant vs. AnyNull interface.
4141         if (ptr == Constant)  ptr = NotNull;   // forget it was a constant
4142         instance_id = InstanceBot;
4143       }
4144       ciObject* o = NULL;  // the Constant value, if any
4145       if (ptr == Constant) {
4146         // Find out which constant.
4147         o = (this_klass == klass()) ? const_oop() : tinst->const_oop();
4148       }
4149       return make(ptr, k, xk, o, off, flat_array, instance_id, speculative, depth);
4150     }
4151 
4152     // Either oop vs oop or interface vs interface or interface vs Object
4153 
4154     // !!! Here's how the symmetry requirement breaks down into invariants:
4155     // If we split one up & one down AND they subtype, take the down man.
4156     // If we split one up & one down AND they do NOT subtype, "fall hard".
4157     // If both are up and they subtype, take the subtype class.
4158     // If both are up and they do NOT subtype, "fall hard".
4159     // If both are down and they subtype, take the supertype class.
4160     // If both are down and they do NOT subtype, "fall hard".
4161     // Constants treated as down.
4162 
4163     // Now, reorder the above list; observe that both-down+subtype is also
4164     // "fall hard"; "fall hard" becomes the default case:
4165     // If we split one up & one down AND they subtype, take the down man.
4166     // If both are up and they subtype, take the subtype class.
4167 
4168     // If both are down and they subtype, "fall hard".
4169     // If both are down and they do NOT subtype, "fall hard".
4170     // If both are up and they do NOT subtype, "fall hard".
4171     // If we split one up & one down AND they do NOT subtype, "fall hard".
4172 
4173     // If a proper subtype is exact, and we return it, we return it exactly.
4174     // If a proper supertype is exact, there can be no subtyping relationship!
4175     // If both types are equal to the subtype, exactness is and-ed below the
4176     // centerline and or-ed above it.  (N.B. Constants are always exact.)
4177 
4178     // Check for subtyping:
4179     ciKlass *subtype = NULL;
4180     bool subtype_exact = false;
4181     bool flat_array = false;
4182     if (tinst_klass->equals(this_klass)) {
4183       subtype = this_klass;
4184       subtype_exact = below_centerline(ptr) ? (this_xk && tinst_xk) : (this_xk || tinst_xk);
4185       flat_array = below_centerline(ptr) ? (this_flat_array && tinst_flat_array) : (this_flat_array || tinst_flat_array);
4186     } else if(!tinst_xk && this_klass->is_subtype_of(tinst_klass) && (!tinst_flat_array || this_flat_array)) {
4187       subtype = this_klass;     // Pick subtyping class
4188       subtype_exact = this_xk;
4189       flat_array = this_flat_array;
4190     } else if(!this_xk && tinst_klass->is_subtype_of(this_klass) && (!this_flat_array || tinst_flat_array)) {
4191       subtype = tinst_klass;    // Pick subtyping class
4192       subtype_exact = tinst_xk;
4193       flat_array = tinst_flat_array;
4194     }
4195 
4196     if (subtype) {
4197       if (above_centerline(ptr)) { // both are up?
4198         this_klass = tinst_klass = subtype;
4199         this_xk = tinst_xk = subtype_exact;
4200         this_flat_array = tinst_flat_array = flat_array;
4201       } else if (above_centerline(this ->_ptr) && !above_centerline(tinst->_ptr)) {
4202         this_klass = tinst_klass; // tinst is down; keep down man
4203         this_xk = tinst_xk;
4204         this_flat_array = tinst_flat_array;
4205       } else if (above_centerline(tinst->_ptr) && !above_centerline(this ->_ptr)) {
4206         tinst_klass = this_klass; // this is down; keep down man
4207         tinst_xk = this_xk;
4208         tinst_flat_array = this_flat_array;
4209       } else {
4210         this_xk = subtype_exact;  // either they are equal, or we'll do an LCA
4211         this_flat_array = flat_array;
4212       }
4213     }
4214 
4215     // Check for classes now being equal
4216     if (tinst_klass->equals(this_klass)) {
4217       // If the klasses are equal, the constants may still differ.  Fall to
4218       // NotNull if they do (neither constant is NULL; that is a special case
4219       // handled elsewhere).
4220       ciObject* o = NULL;             // Assume not constant when done
4221       ciObject* this_oop  = const_oop();
4222       ciObject* tinst_oop = tinst->const_oop();
4223       if( ptr == Constant ) {
4224         if (this_oop != NULL && tinst_oop != NULL &&
4225             this_oop->equals(tinst_oop) )
4226           o = this_oop;
4227         else if (above_centerline(this ->_ptr))
4228           o = tinst_oop;
4229         else if (above_centerline(tinst ->_ptr))
4230           o = this_oop;
4231         else
4232           ptr = NotNull;
4233       }
4234       return make(ptr, this_klass, this_xk, o, off, this_flat_array, instance_id, speculative, depth);
4235     } // Else classes are not equal
4236 
4237     // Since klasses are different, we require a LCA in the Java
4238     // class hierarchy - which means we have to fall to at least NotNull.
4239     if( ptr == TopPTR || ptr == AnyNull || ptr == Constant )
4240       ptr = NotNull;
4241 
4242     instance_id = InstanceBot;
4243 
4244     // Now we find the LCA of Java classes
4245     ciKlass* k = this_klass->least_common_ancestor(tinst_klass);
4246     return make(ptr, k, false, NULL, off, false, instance_id, speculative, depth);
4247   } // End of case InstPtr
4248 
4249   case InlineType: {
4250     const TypeInlineType* tv = t->is_inlinetype();
4251     if (above_centerline(ptr())) {
4252       if (tv->inline_klass()->is_subtype_of(_klass)) {
4253         return t;
4254       } else {
4255         return TypeInstPtr::NOTNULL;
4256       }
4257     } else {
4258       PTR ptr = this->_ptr;
4259       if (ptr == Constant) {
4260         ptr = NotNull;
4261       }
4262       if (tv->inline_klass()->is_subtype_of(_klass)) {
4263         return TypeInstPtr::make(ptr, _klass);
4264       } else {
4265         return TypeInstPtr::make(ptr, ciEnv::current()->Object_klass());
4266       }
4267     }
4268   }
4269 
4270   } // End of switch
4271   return this;                  // Return the double constant
4272 }
4273 
4274 
4275 //------------------------java_mirror_type--------------------------------------
4276 ciType* TypeInstPtr::java_mirror_type() const {
4277   // must be a singleton type
4278   if( const_oop() == NULL )  return NULL;
4279 
4280   // must be of type java.lang.Class
4281   if( klass() != ciEnv::current()->Class_klass() )  return NULL;

4282   return const_oop()->as_instance()->java_mirror_type();
4283 }

4288 // inheritance mechanism.
4289 const Type *TypeInstPtr::xdual() const {
4290   return new TypeInstPtr(dual_ptr(), klass(), klass_is_exact(), const_oop(), dual_offset(), flat_array(), dual_instance_id(), dual_speculative(), dual_inline_depth());
4291 }

4293 //------------------------------eq---------------------------------------------
4294 // Structural equality check for Type representations
4295 bool TypeInstPtr::eq( const Type *t ) const {
4296   const TypeInstPtr *p = t->is_instptr();
4297   return
4298     klass()->equals(p->klass()) &&
4299     flat_array() == p->flat_array() &&
4300     TypeOopPtr::eq(p);          // Check sub-type stuff
4301 }

4303 //------------------------------hash-------------------------------------------
4304 // Type-specific hashing function.
4305 int TypeInstPtr::hash(void) const {
4306   int hash = java_add(java_add((jint)klass()->hash(), (jint)TypeOopPtr::hash()), (jint)flat_array());
4307   return hash;
4308 }

4310 //------------------------------dump2------------------------------------------
4311 // Dump oop Type
4312 #ifndef PRODUCT
4313 void TypeInstPtr::dump2( Dict &d, uint depth, outputStream *st ) const {
4314   // Print the name of the klass.
4315   klass()->print_name_on(st);
4316 
4317   switch( _ptr ) {
4318   case Constant:
4319     // TO DO: Make CI print the hex address of the underlying oop.
4320     if (WizardMode || Verbose) {
4321       const_oop()->print_oop(st);
4322     }
4323   case BotPTR:
4324     if (!WizardMode && !Verbose) {
4325       if( _klass_is_exact ) st->print(":exact");
4326       break;
4327     }
4328   case TopPTR:
4329   case AnyNull:
4330   case NotNull:
4331     st->print(":%s", ptr_msg[_ptr]);
4332     if( _klass_is_exact ) st->print(":exact");
4333     break;
4334   default:
4335     break;
4336   }
4337 
4338   _offset.dump2(st);




4339 
4340   st->print(" *");
4341 
4342   if (flat_array() && !klass()->is_inlinetype()) {
4343     st->print(" (flatten array)");
4344   }
4345 
4346   if (_instance_id == InstanceTop)
4347     st->print(",iid=top");
4348   else if (_instance_id != InstanceBot)
4349     st->print(",iid=%d",_instance_id);
4350 
4351   dump_inline_depth(st);
4352   dump_speculative(st);
4353 }
4354 #endif

4359               _instance_id, add_offset_speculative(offset), _inline_depth);

4362 const Type *TypeInstPtr::remove_speculative() const {
4363   if (_speculative == NULL) {
4364     return this;
4365   }
4366   assert(_inline_depth == InlineDepthTop || _inline_depth == InlineDepthBottom, "non speculative type shouldn't have inline depth");
4367   return make(_ptr, klass(), klass_is_exact(), const_oop(), _offset, flat_array(),
4368               _instance_id, NULL, _inline_depth);
4369 }

4372   if (!UseInlineDepthForSpeculativeTypes) {
4373     return this;
4374   }

4376 }

4381 }

4402 //------------------------------make-------------------------------------------
4403 const TypeAryPtr* TypeAryPtr::make(PTR ptr, const TypeAry *ary, ciKlass* k, bool xk, Offset offset, Offset field_offset,
4404                                    int instance_id, const TypePtr* speculative, int inline_depth) {
4405   assert(!(k == NULL && ary->_elem->isa_int()),
4406          "integral arrays must be pre-equipped with a class");
4407   if (!xk)  xk = ary->ary_must_be_exact();
4408   assert(instance_id <= 0 || xk, "instances are always exactly typed");
4409   return (TypeAryPtr*)(new TypeAryPtr(ptr, NULL, ary, k, xk, offset, field_offset, instance_id, false, speculative, inline_depth))->hashcons();
4410 }
4411 
4412 //------------------------------make-------------------------------------------
4413 const TypeAryPtr* TypeAryPtr::make(PTR ptr, ciObject* o, const TypeAry *ary, ciKlass* k, bool xk, Offset offset, Offset field_offset,
4414                                    int instance_id, const TypePtr* speculative, int inline_depth,
4415                                    bool is_autobox_cache) {
4416   assert(!(k == NULL && ary->_elem->isa_int()),
4417          "integral arrays must be pre-equipped with a class");
4418   assert( (ptr==Constant && o) || (ptr!=Constant && !o), "" );
4419   if (!xk)  xk = (o != NULL) || ary->ary_must_be_exact();
4420   assert(instance_id <= 0 || xk, "instances are always exactly typed");
4421   return (TypeAryPtr*)(new TypeAryPtr(ptr, o, ary, k, xk, offset, field_offset, instance_id, is_autobox_cache, speculative, inline_depth))->hashcons();
4422 }

4424 //------------------------------cast_to_ptr_type-------------------------------
4425 const Type *TypeAryPtr::cast_to_ptr_type(PTR ptr) const {
4426   if( ptr == _ptr ) return this;
4427   return make(ptr, const_oop(), _ary, klass(), klass_is_exact(), _offset, _field_offset, _instance_id, _speculative, _inline_depth, _is_autobox_cache);
4428 }
4429 
4430 
4431 //-----------------------------cast_to_exactness-------------------------------
4432 const Type *TypeAryPtr::cast_to_exactness(bool klass_is_exact) const {
4433   if( klass_is_exact == _klass_is_exact ) return this;
4434   if (_ary->ary_must_be_exact())  return this;  // cannot clear xk
4435 
4436   const TypeAry* new_ary = _ary;
4437   if (klass() != NULL && klass()->is_obj_array_klass() && klass_is_exact) {
4438     // An object array can't be flat or null-free if the klass is exact
4439     new_ary = TypeAry::make(elem(), size(), is_stable(), /* not_flat= */ true, /* not_null_free= */ true);
4440   }
4441   return make(ptr(), const_oop(), new_ary, klass(), klass_is_exact, _offset, _field_offset, _instance_id, _speculative, _inline_depth, _is_autobox_cache);
4442 }
4443 
4444 //-----------------------------cast_to_instance_id----------------------------
4445 const TypeOopPtr *TypeAryPtr::cast_to_instance_id(int instance_id) const {
4446   if( instance_id == _instance_id ) return this;
4447   return make(_ptr, const_oop(), _ary, klass(), _klass_is_exact, _offset, _field_offset, instance_id, _speculative, _inline_depth, _is_autobox_cache);
4448 }

4451 //-----------------------------max_array_length-------------------------------
4452 // A wrapper around arrayOopDesc::max_array_length(etype) with some input normalization.
4453 jint TypeAryPtr::max_array_length(BasicType etype) {
4454   if (!is_java_primitive(etype) && !is_reference_type(etype)) {
4455     if (etype == T_NARROWOOP) {
4456       etype = T_OBJECT;
4457     } else if (etype == T_ILLEGAL) { // bottom[]
4458       etype = T_BYTE; // will produce conservatively high value
4459     } else {
4460       fatal("not an element type: %s", type2name(etype));
4461     }
4462   }
4463   return arrayOopDesc::max_array_length(etype);
4464 }
4465 
4466 //-----------------------------narrow_size_type-------------------------------
4467 // Narrow the given size type to the index range for the given array base type.

4483   if (hi > max_hi) {
4484     hi = max_hi;
4485     if (size->is_con()) {
4486       lo = hi;
4487     }
4488     chg = true;
4489   }
4490   // Negative length arrays will produce weird intermediate dead fast-path code
4491   if (lo > hi)
4492     return TypeInt::ZERO;
4493   if (!chg)
4494     return size;
4495   return TypeInt::make(lo, hi, Type::WidenMin);
4496 }
4497 
4498 //-------------------------------cast_to_size----------------------------------
4499 const TypeAryPtr* TypeAryPtr::cast_to_size(const TypeInt* new_size) const {
4500   assert(new_size != NULL, "");
4501   new_size = narrow_size_type(new_size);
4502   if (new_size == size())  return this;
4503   const TypeAry* new_ary = TypeAry::make(elem(), new_size, is_stable(), is_not_flat(), is_not_null_free());
4504   return make(ptr(), const_oop(), new_ary, klass(), klass_is_exact(), _offset, _field_offset, _instance_id, _speculative, _inline_depth, _is_autobox_cache);
4505 }
4506 
4507 //-------------------------------cast_to_not_flat------------------------------
4508 const TypeAryPtr* TypeAryPtr::cast_to_not_flat(bool not_flat) const {
4509   if (not_flat == is_not_flat()) {
4510     return this;
4511   }
4512   const TypeAry* new_ary = TypeAry::make(elem(), size(), is_stable(), not_flat, is_not_null_free());
4513   return make(ptr(), const_oop(), new_ary, klass(), klass_is_exact(), _offset, _field_offset, _instance_id, _speculative, _inline_depth, _is_autobox_cache);
4514 }
4515 
4516 //-------------------------------cast_to_not_null_free-------------------------
4517 const TypeAryPtr* TypeAryPtr::cast_to_not_null_free(bool not_null_free) const {
4518   if (not_null_free == is_not_null_free()) {
4519     return this;
4520   }
4521   // Not null free implies not flat
4522   const TypeAry* new_ary = TypeAry::make(elem(), size(), is_stable(), not_null_free ? true : is_not_flat(), not_null_free);
4523   return make(ptr(), const_oop(), new_ary, klass(), klass_is_exact(), _offset, _field_offset, _instance_id, _speculative, _inline_depth, _is_autobox_cache);
4524 }
4525 
4526 //------------------------------cast_to_stable---------------------------------
4527 const TypeAryPtr* TypeAryPtr::cast_to_stable(bool stable, int stable_dimension) const {
4528   if (stable_dimension <= 0 || (stable_dimension == 1 && stable == this->is_stable()))
4529     return this;
4530 
4531   const Type* elem = this->elem();
4532   const TypePtr* elem_ptr = elem->make_ptr();
4533 
4534   if (stable_dimension > 1 && elem_ptr != NULL && elem_ptr->isa_aryptr()) {
4535     // If this is widened from a narrow oop, TypeAry::make will re-narrow it.
4536     elem = elem_ptr = elem_ptr->is_aryptr()->cast_to_stable(stable, stable_dimension - 1);
4537   }
4538 
4539   const TypeAry* new_ary = TypeAry::make(elem, size(), stable, is_not_flat(), is_not_null_free());
4540 
4541   return make(ptr(), const_oop(), new_ary, klass(), klass_is_exact(), _offset, _field_offset, _instance_id, _speculative, _inline_depth, _is_autobox_cache);
4542 }
4543 
4544 //-----------------------------stable_dimension--------------------------------
4545 int TypeAryPtr::stable_dimension() const {
4546   if (!is_stable())  return 0;
4547   int dim = 1;
4548   const TypePtr* elem_ptr = elem()->make_ptr();
4549   if (elem_ptr != NULL && elem_ptr->isa_aryptr())
4550     dim += elem_ptr->is_aryptr()->stable_dimension();
4551   return dim;
4552 }
4553 
4554 //----------------------cast_to_autobox_cache-----------------------------------
4555 const TypeAryPtr* TypeAryPtr::cast_to_autobox_cache(bool cache) const {
4556   if (is_autobox_cache() == cache)  return this;
4557   const TypeOopPtr* etype = elem()->make_oopptr();
4558   if (etype == NULL)  return this;
4559   // The pointers in the autobox arrays are always non-null.
4560   TypePtr::PTR ptr_type = cache ? TypePtr::NotNull : TypePtr::AnyNull;
4561   etype = etype->cast_to_ptr_type(TypePtr::NotNull)->is_oopptr();
4562   const TypeAry* new_ary = TypeAry::make(etype, size(), is_stable(), is_not_flat(), is_not_null_free());
4563   return make(ptr(), const_oop(), new_ary, klass(), klass_is_exact(), _offset, _field_offset, _instance_id, _speculative, _inline_depth, cache);
4564 }
4565 
4566 //------------------------------eq---------------------------------------------
4567 // Structural equality check for Type representations
4568 bool TypeAryPtr::eq( const Type *t ) const {
4569   const TypeAryPtr *p = t->is_aryptr();
4570   return
4571     _ary == p->_ary &&  // Check array
4572     TypeOopPtr::eq(p) &&// Check sub-parts
4573     _field_offset == p->_field_offset;
4574 }
4575 
4576 //------------------------------hash-------------------------------------------
4577 // Type-specific hashing function.
4578 int TypeAryPtr::hash(void) const {
4579   return (intptr_t)_ary + TypeOopPtr::hash() + _field_offset.get();
4580 }
4581 
4582 //------------------------------meet-------------------------------------------
4583 // Compute the MEET of two types.  It returns a new Type object.
4584 const Type *TypeAryPtr::xmeet_helper(const Type *t) const {
4585   // Perform a fast test for common case; meeting the same types together.
4586   if( this == t ) return this;  // Meeting same type-rep?
4587   // Current "this->_base" is Pointer
4588   switch (t->base()) {          // switch on original type
4589 
4590   // Mixing ints & oops happens when javac reuses local variables
4591   case Int:
4592   case Long:
4593   case FloatTop:
4594   case FloatCon:
4595   case FloatBot:
4596   case DoubleTop:
4597   case DoubleCon:
4598   case DoubleBot:
4599   case NarrowOop:
4600   case NarrowKlass:
4601   case Bottom:                  // Ye Olde Default
4602     return Type::BOTTOM;
4603   case Top:
4604     return this;
4605 
4606   default:                      // All else is a mistake
4607     typerr(t);
4608 
4609   case OopPtr: {                // Meeting to OopPtrs
4610     // Found a OopPtr type vs self-AryPtr type
4611     const TypeOopPtr *tp = t->is_oopptr();
4612     Offset offset = meet_offset(tp->offset());
4613     PTR ptr = meet_ptr(tp->ptr());
4614     int depth = meet_inline_depth(tp->inline_depth());
4615     const TypePtr* speculative = xmeet_speculative(tp);
4616     switch (tp->ptr()) {
4617     case TopPTR:
4618     case AnyNull: {
4619       int instance_id = meet_instance_id(InstanceTop);
4620       return make(ptr, (ptr == Constant ? const_oop() : NULL),
4621                   _ary, _klass, _klass_is_exact, offset, _field_offset, instance_id, speculative, depth);
4622     }
4623     case BotPTR:
4624     case NotNull: {
4625       int instance_id = meet_instance_id(tp->instance_id());
4626       return TypeOopPtr::make(ptr, offset, instance_id, speculative, depth);
4627     }
4628     default: ShouldNotReachHere();
4629     }
4630   }
4631 
4632   case AnyPtr: {                // Meeting two AnyPtrs
4633     // Found an AnyPtr type vs self-AryPtr type
4634     const TypePtr *tp = t->is_ptr();
4635     Offset offset = meet_offset(tp->offset());
4636     PTR ptr = meet_ptr(tp->ptr());
4637     const TypePtr* speculative = xmeet_speculative(tp);
4638     int depth = meet_inline_depth(tp->inline_depth());
4639     switch (tp->ptr()) {
4640     case TopPTR:
4641       return this;
4642     case BotPTR:
4643     case NotNull:
4644       return TypePtr::make(AnyPtr, ptr, offset, speculative, depth);
4645     case Null:
4646       if( ptr == Null ) return TypePtr::make(AnyPtr, ptr, offset, speculative, depth);
4647       // else fall through to AnyNull
4648     case AnyNull: {
4649       int instance_id = meet_instance_id(InstanceTop);
4650       return make(ptr, (ptr == Constant ? const_oop() : NULL),
4651                   _ary, _klass, _klass_is_exact, offset, _field_offset, instance_id, speculative, depth);
4652     }
4653     default: ShouldNotReachHere();
4654     }
4655   }
4656 
4657   case MetadataPtr:
4658   case KlassPtr:
4659   case RawPtr: return TypePtr::BOTTOM;
4660 
4661   case AryPtr: {                // Meeting 2 references?
4662     const TypeAryPtr *tap = t->is_aryptr();
4663     Offset off = meet_offset(tap->offset());
4664     Offset field_off = meet_field_offset(tap->field_offset());
4665     const TypeAry *tary = _ary->meet_speculative(tap->_ary)->is_ary();
4666     PTR ptr = meet_ptr(tap->ptr());
4667     int instance_id = meet_instance_id(tap->instance_id());
4668     const TypePtr* speculative = xmeet_speculative(tap);
4669     int depth = meet_inline_depth(tap->inline_depth());
4670     ciKlass* lazy_klass = NULL;
4671     if (tary->_elem->isa_int()) {
4672       // Integral array element types have irrelevant lattice relations.
4673       // It is the klass that determines array layout, not the element type.
4674       if (_klass == NULL)
4675         lazy_klass = tap->_klass;
4676       else if (tap->_klass == NULL || tap->_klass == _klass) {
4677         lazy_klass = _klass;
4678       } else {
4679         // Something like byte[int+] meets char[int+].
4680         // This must fall to bottom, not (int[-128..65535])[int+].
4681         instance_id = InstanceBot;
4682         tary = TypeAry::make(Type::BOTTOM, tary->_size, tary->_stable, tary->_not_flat, tary->_not_null_free);
4683       }
4684     } else // Non integral arrays.
4685       // Must fall to bottom if exact klasses in upper lattice
4686       // are not equal or super klass is exact.
4687       if ((above_centerline(ptr) || ptr == Constant) && klass() != tap->klass() &&
4688           // meet with top[] and bottom[] are processed further down:
4689           tap->_klass != NULL && this->_klass != NULL &&
4690           // both are exact and not equal:
4691           ((tap->_klass_is_exact && this->_klass_is_exact) ||
4692            // 'tap' is exact and super or unrelated:
4693            (tap->_klass_is_exact && !tap->klass()->is_subtype_of(klass())) ||
4694            // 'this' is exact and super or unrelated:
4695            (this->_klass_is_exact && !klass()->is_subtype_of(tap->klass())))) {
4696       if (above_centerline(ptr) || (tary->_elem->make_ptr() && above_centerline(tary->_elem->make_ptr()->_ptr))) {
4697         tary = TypeAry::make(Type::BOTTOM, tary->_size, tary->_stable, tary->_not_flat, tary->_not_null_free);
4698       }
4699       return make(NotNull, NULL, tary, lazy_klass, false, off, field_off, InstanceBot, speculative, depth);
4700     } else if (klass() != NULL && tap->klass() != NULL && klass()->is_flat_array_klass() != tap->klass()->is_flat_array_klass()) {
4701       // Meeting flattened inline type array with non-flattened array. Adjust (field) offset accordingly.
4702       if (tary->_elem->isa_inlinetype()) {
4703         // Result is flattened
4704         off = Offset(elem()->isa_inlinetype() ? offset() : tap->offset());
4705         field_off = elem()->isa_inlinetype() ? field_offset() : tap->field_offset();
4706       } else if (tary->_elem->make_oopptr() != NULL && tary->_elem->make_oopptr()->isa_instptr() && below_centerline(ptr)) {
4707         // Result is non-flattened
4708         off = Offset(flattened_offset()).meet(Offset(tap->flattened_offset()));
4709         field_off = Offset::bottom;
4710       }

4711     }
4712 
4713     bool xk = false;
4714     switch (tap->ptr()) {
4715     case AnyNull:
4716     case TopPTR:
4717       // Compute new klass on demand, do not use tap->_klass
4718       if (below_centerline(this->_ptr)) {
4719         xk = this->_klass_is_exact;
4720       } else {
4721         xk = (tap->_klass_is_exact || this->_klass_is_exact);
4722       }
4723       return make(ptr, const_oop(), tary, lazy_klass, xk, off, field_off, instance_id, speculative, depth);
4724     case Constant: {
4725       ciObject* o = const_oop();
4726       if( _ptr == Constant ) {
4727         if( tap->const_oop() != NULL && !o->equals(tap->const_oop()) ) {
4728           xk = (klass() == tap->klass());
4729           ptr = NotNull;
4730           o = NULL;
4731           instance_id = InstanceBot;
4732         } else {
4733           xk = true;
4734         }
4735       } else if(above_centerline(_ptr)) {
4736         o = tap->const_oop();
4737         xk = true;
4738       } else {
4739         // Only precise for identical arrays
4740         xk = this->_klass_is_exact && (klass() == tap->klass());
4741       }
4742       return TypeAryPtr::make(ptr, o, tary, lazy_klass, xk, off, field_off, instance_id, speculative, depth);
4743     }
4744     case NotNull:
4745     case BotPTR:
4746       // Compute new klass on demand, do not use tap->_klass
4747       if (above_centerline(this->_ptr))
4748             xk = tap->_klass_is_exact;
4749       else  xk = (tap->_klass_is_exact & this->_klass_is_exact) &&
4750               (klass() == tap->klass()); // Only precise for identical arrays
4751       return TypeAryPtr::make(ptr, NULL, tary, lazy_klass, xk, off, field_off, instance_id, speculative, depth);
4752     default: ShouldNotReachHere();
4753     }
4754   }
4755 
4756   // All arrays inherit from Object class
4757   case InstPtr: {
4758     const TypeInstPtr *tp = t->is_instptr();
4759     Offset offset = meet_offset(tp->offset());
4760     PTR ptr = meet_ptr(tp->ptr());
4761     int instance_id = meet_instance_id(tp->instance_id());
4762     const TypePtr* speculative = xmeet_speculative(tp);
4763     int depth = meet_inline_depth(tp->inline_depth());
4764     switch (ptr) {
4765     case TopPTR:
4766     case AnyNull:                // Fall 'down' to dual of object klass
4767       // For instances when a subclass meets a superclass we fall
4768       // below the centerline when the superclass is exact. We need to
4769       // do the same here.
4770       if (tp->klass()->equals(ciEnv::current()->Object_klass()) && !tp->klass_is_exact() && !tp->flat_array()) {
4771         return TypeAryPtr::make(ptr, _ary, _klass, _klass_is_exact, offset, _field_offset, instance_id, speculative, depth);
4772       } else {
4773         // cannot subclass, so the meet has to fall badly below the centerline
4774         ptr = NotNull;
4775         instance_id = InstanceBot;
4776         return TypeInstPtr::make(ptr, ciEnv::current()->Object_klass(), false, NULL, offset, false, instance_id, speculative, depth);
4777       }
4778     case Constant:
4779     case NotNull:
4780     case BotPTR:                // Fall down to object klass
4781       // LCA is object_klass, but if we subclass from the top we can do better
4782       if (above_centerline(tp->ptr())) {
4783         // If 'tp'  is above the centerline and it is Object class
4784         // then we can subclass in the Java class hierarchy.
4785         // For instances when a subclass meets a superclass we fall
4786         // below the centerline when the superclass is exact. We need
4787         // to do the same here.
4788         if (tp->klass()->equals(ciEnv::current()->Object_klass()) && !tp->klass_is_exact() && !tp->flat_array()) {
4789           // that is, my array type is a subtype of 'tp' klass
4790           return make(ptr, (ptr == Constant ? const_oop() : NULL),
4791                       _ary, _klass, _klass_is_exact, offset, _field_offset, instance_id, speculative, depth);
4792         }
4793       }
4794       // The other case cannot happen, since t cannot be a subtype of an array.
4795       // The meet falls down to Object class below centerline.
4796       if( ptr == Constant )
4797          ptr = NotNull;
4798       instance_id = InstanceBot;
4799       return TypeInstPtr::make(ptr, ciEnv::current()->Object_klass(), false, NULL, offset, false, instance_id, speculative, depth);
4800     default: typerr(t);
4801     }
4802   }
4803 
4804   case InlineType: {
4805     const TypeInlineType* tv = t->is_inlinetype();
4806     if (above_centerline(ptr())) {
4807       return TypeInstPtr::NOTNULL;
4808     } else {
4809       PTR ptr = this->_ptr;
4810       if (ptr == Constant) {
4811         ptr = NotNull;
4812       }
4813       return TypeInstPtr::make(ptr, ciEnv::current()->Object_klass());
4814     }
4815   }
4816   }
4817   return this;                  // Lint noise
4818 }
4819 
4820 //------------------------------xdual------------------------------------------
4821 // Dual: compute field-by-field dual
4822 const Type *TypeAryPtr::xdual() const {
4823   return new TypeAryPtr(dual_ptr(), _const_oop, _ary->dual()->is_ary(), _klass, _klass_is_exact, dual_offset(), dual_field_offset(), dual_instance_id(), is_autobox_cache(), dual_speculative(), dual_inline_depth());
4824 }
4825 
4826 Type::Offset TypeAryPtr::meet_field_offset(const Type::Offset offset) const {
4827   return _field_offset.meet(offset);
4828 }
4829 
4830 //------------------------------dual_offset------------------------------------
4831 Type::Offset TypeAryPtr::dual_field_offset() const {
4832   return _field_offset.dual();
4833 }

4836 #ifdef ASSERT
4837 bool TypeAryPtr::interface_vs_oop(const Type *t) const {
4838   const TypeAryPtr* t_aryptr = t->isa_aryptr();
4839   if (t_aryptr) {
4840     return _ary->interface_vs_oop(t_aryptr->_ary);
4841   }
4842   return false;

4846 //------------------------------dump2------------------------------------------
4847 #ifndef PRODUCT
4848 void TypeAryPtr::dump2( Dict &d, uint depth, outputStream *st ) const {
4849   _ary->dump2(d,depth,st);
4850   switch( _ptr ) {
4851   case Constant:
4852     const_oop()->print(st);
4853     break;
4854   case BotPTR:
4855     if (!WizardMode && !Verbose) {
4856       if( _klass_is_exact ) st->print(":exact");
4857       break;
4858     }
4859   case TopPTR:
4860   case AnyNull:
4861   case NotNull:
4862     st->print(":%s", ptr_msg[_ptr]);
4863     if( _klass_is_exact ) st->print(":exact");
4864     break;
4865   default:
4866     break;
4867   }
4868 
4869   if (elem()->isa_inlinetype()) {
4870     st->print("(");
4871     _field_offset.dump2(st);
4872     st->print(")");
4873   }
4874   if (offset() != 0) {
4875     int header_size = objArrayOopDesc::header_size() * wordSize;
4876     if( _offset == Offset::top )       st->print("+undefined");
4877     else if( _offset == Offset::bottom )  st->print("+any");
4878     else if( offset() < header_size ) st->print("+%d", offset());
4879     else {
4880       BasicType basic_elem_type = elem()->basic_type();
4881       int array_base = arrayOopDesc::base_offset_in_bytes(basic_elem_type);
4882       int elem_size = type2aelembytes(basic_elem_type);
4883       st->print("[%d]", (offset() - array_base)/elem_size);
4884     }
4885   }
4886   st->print(" *");
4887   if (_instance_id == InstanceTop)
4888     st->print(",iid=top");
4889   else if (_instance_id != InstanceBot)
4890     st->print(",iid=%d",_instance_id);
4891 
4892   dump_inline_depth(st);
4893   dump_speculative(st);
4894 }
4895 #endif
4896 
4897 bool TypeAryPtr::empty(void) const {
4898   if (_ary->empty())       return true;
4899   return TypeOopPtr::empty();
4900 }
4901 
4902 //------------------------------add_offset-------------------------------------
4903 const TypePtr *TypeAryPtr::add_offset(intptr_t offset) const {
4904   return make(_ptr, _const_oop, _ary, _klass, _klass_is_exact, xadd_offset(offset), _field_offset, _instance_id, add_offset_speculative(offset), _inline_depth, _is_autobox_cache);
4905 }
4906 
4907 const Type *TypeAryPtr::remove_speculative() const {
4908   if (_speculative == NULL) {
4909     return this;
4910   }
4911   assert(_inline_depth == InlineDepthTop || _inline_depth == InlineDepthBottom, "non speculative type shouldn't have inline depth");
4912   return make(_ptr, _const_oop, _ary->remove_speculative()->is_ary(), _klass, _klass_is_exact, _offset, _field_offset, _instance_id, NULL, _inline_depth, _is_autobox_cache);
4913 }
4914 
4915 const Type* TypeAryPtr::cleanup_speculative() const {
4916   if (speculative() == NULL) {
4917     return this;
4918   }
4919   // Keep speculative part if it contains information about flat-/nullability
4920   const TypeAryPtr* spec_aryptr = speculative()->isa_aryptr();
4921   if (spec_aryptr != NULL && (spec_aryptr->is_not_flat() || spec_aryptr->is_not_null_free())) {
4922     return this;
4923   }
4924   return TypeOopPtr::cleanup_speculative();
4925 }
4926 
4927 const TypePtr *TypeAryPtr::with_inline_depth(int depth) const {
4928   if (!UseInlineDepthForSpeculativeTypes) {
4929     return this;
4930   }
4931   return make(_ptr, _const_oop, _ary->remove_speculative()->is_ary(), _klass, _klass_is_exact, _offset, _field_offset, _instance_id, _speculative, depth, _is_autobox_cache);
4932 }
4933 
4934 const TypeAryPtr* TypeAryPtr::with_field_offset(int offset) const {
4935   return make(_ptr, _const_oop, _ary->remove_speculative()->is_ary(), _klass, _klass_is_exact, _offset, Offset(offset), _instance_id, _speculative, _inline_depth, _is_autobox_cache);
4936 }
4937 
4938 const TypePtr* TypeAryPtr::add_field_offset_and_offset(intptr_t offset) const {
4939   int adj = 0;
4940   if (offset != Type::OffsetBot && offset != Type::OffsetTop) {
4941     const Type* elemtype = elem();
4942     if (elemtype->isa_inlinetype()) {
4943       if (_offset.get() != OffsetBot && _offset.get() != OffsetTop) {
4944         adj = _offset.get();
4945         offset += _offset.get();
4946       }
4947       uint header = arrayOopDesc::base_offset_in_bytes(T_OBJECT);
4948       if (_field_offset.get() != OffsetBot && _field_offset.get() != OffsetTop) {
4949         offset += _field_offset.get();
4950         if (_offset.get() == OffsetBot || _offset.get() == OffsetTop) {
4951           offset += header;
4952         }
4953       }
4954       if (offset >= (intptr_t)header || offset < 0) {
4955         // Try to get the field of the inline type array element we are pointing to
4956         ciKlass* arytype_klass = klass();
4957         ciFlatArrayKlass* vak = arytype_klass->as_flat_array_klass();
4958         ciInlineKlass* vk = vak->element_klass()->as_inline_klass();
4959         int shift = vak->log2_element_size();
4960         int mask = (1 << shift) - 1;
4961         intptr_t field_offset = ((offset - header) & mask);
4962         ciField* field = vk->get_field_by_offset(field_offset + vk->first_field_offset(), false);
4963         if (field == NULL) {
4964           // This may happen with nested AddP(base, AddP(base, base, offset), longcon(16))
4965           return add_offset(offset);
4966         } else {
4967           return with_field_offset(field_offset)->add_offset(offset - field_offset - adj);
4968         }
4969       }
4970     }
4971   }
4972   return add_offset(offset - adj);
4973 }
4974 
4975 // Return offset incremented by field_offset for flattened inline type arrays
4976 const int TypeAryPtr::flattened_offset() const {
4977   int offset = _offset.get();
4978   if (offset != Type::OffsetBot && offset != Type::OffsetTop &&
4979       _field_offset != Offset::bottom && _field_offset != Offset::top) {
4980     offset += _field_offset.get();
4981   }
4982   return offset;
4983 }
4984 
4985 const TypePtr *TypeAryPtr::with_instance_id(int instance_id) const {
4986   assert(is_known_instance(), "should be known");
4987   return make(_ptr, _const_oop, _ary->remove_speculative()->is_ary(), _klass, _klass_is_exact, _offset, _field_offset, instance_id, _speculative, _inline_depth);
4988 }

5010 
5011 bool TypeNarrowPtr::eq( const Type *t ) const {
5012   const TypeNarrowPtr* tc = isa_same_narrowptr(t);

5061   // Current "this->_base" is NarrowKlass or NarrowOop
5062   switch (t->base()) {          // switch on original type
5063 
5064   case Int:                     // Mixing ints & oops happens when javac
5065   case Long:                    // reuses local variables
5066   case FloatTop:
5067   case FloatCon:
5068   case FloatBot:
5069   case DoubleTop:
5070   case DoubleCon:
5071   case DoubleBot:
5072   case AnyPtr:
5073   case RawPtr:
5074   case OopPtr:
5075   case InstPtr:
5076   case AryPtr:
5077   case MetadataPtr:
5078   case KlassPtr:
5079   case NarrowOop:
5080   case NarrowKlass:

5081   case Bottom:                  // Ye Olde Default
5082     return Type::BOTTOM;
5083   case Top:
5084     return this;
5085 
5086   case InlineType:
5087     return t->xmeet(this);
5088 
5089   default:                      // All else is a mistake
5090     typerr(t);
5091 
5092   } // End of switch
5093 
5094   return this;
5095 }

5099   _ptrtype->dump2(d, depth, st);
5100 }

5107 const TypeNarrowOop* TypeNarrowOop::make(const TypePtr* type) {
5108   return (const TypeNarrowOop*)(new TypeNarrowOop(type))->hashcons();

5147     return (one == two) && TypePtr::eq(t);
5148   } else {
5149     return one->equals(two) && TypePtr::eq(t);
5150   }
5151 }

5153 //------------------------------hash-------------------------------------------
5154 // Type-specific hashing function.
5155 int TypeMetadataPtr::hash(void) const {
5156   return
5157     (metadata() ? metadata()->hash() : 0) +
5158     TypePtr::hash();
5159 }

5161 //------------------------------singleton--------------------------------------
5162 // TRUE if Type is a singleton type, FALSE otherwise.   Singletons are simple
5163 // constants
5164 bool TypeMetadataPtr::singleton(void) const {
5165   // detune optimizer to not generate constant metadata + constant offset as a constant!
5166   // TopPTR, Null, AnyNull, Constant are all singletons
5167   return (offset() == 0) && !below_centerline(_ptr);
5168 }
5169 
5170 //------------------------------add_offset-------------------------------------
5171 const TypePtr *TypeMetadataPtr::add_offset( intptr_t offset ) const {
5172   return make( _ptr, _metadata, xadd_offset(offset));
5173 }
5174 
5175 //-----------------------------filter------------------------------------------
5176 // Do not allow interface-vs.-noninterface joins to collapse to top.
5177 const Type *TypeMetadataPtr::filter_helper(const Type *kills, bool include_speculative) const {
5178   const TypeMetadataPtr* ft = join_helper(kills, include_speculative)->isa_metadataptr();
5179   if (ft == NULL || ft->empty())
5180     return Type::TOP;           // Canonical empty value
5181   return ft;
5182 }
5183 
5184  //------------------------------get_con----------------------------------------
5185 intptr_t TypeMetadataPtr::get_con() const {
5186   assert( _ptr == Null || _ptr == Constant, "" );
5187   assert(offset() >= 0, "");
5188 
5189   if (offset() != 0) {
5190     // After being ported to the compiler interface, the compiler no longer
5191     // directly manipulates the addresses of oops.  Rather, it only has a pointer
5192     // to a handle at compile time.  This handle is embedded in the generated
5193     // code and dereferenced at the time the nmethod is made.  Until that time,
5194     // it is not reasonable to do arithmetic with the addresses of oops (we don't
5195     // have access to the addresses!).  This does not seem to currently happen,
5196     // but this assertion here is to help prevent its occurence.
5197     tty->print_cr("Found oop constant with non-zero offset");
5198     ShouldNotReachHere();
5199   }
5200 
5201   return (intptr_t)metadata()->constant_encoding();
5202 }
5203 
5204 //------------------------------cast_to_ptr_type-------------------------------
5205 const Type *TypeMetadataPtr::cast_to_ptr_type(PTR ptr) const {
5206   if( ptr == _ptr ) return this;
5207   return make(ptr, metadata(), _offset);
5208 }
5209 

5220   case Long:                    // reuses local variables
5221   case FloatTop:
5222   case FloatCon:
5223   case FloatBot:
5224   case DoubleTop:
5225   case DoubleCon:
5226   case DoubleBot:
5227   case NarrowOop:
5228   case NarrowKlass:
5229   case Bottom:                  // Ye Olde Default
5230     return Type::BOTTOM;
5231   case Top:
5232     return this;
5233 
5234   default:                      // All else is a mistake
5235     typerr(t);
5236 
5237   case AnyPtr: {
5238     // Found an AnyPtr type vs self-OopPtr type
5239     const TypePtr *tp = t->is_ptr();
5240     Offset offset = meet_offset(tp->offset());
5241     PTR ptr = meet_ptr(tp->ptr());
5242     switch (tp->ptr()) {
5243     case Null:
5244       if (ptr == Null)  return TypePtr::make(AnyPtr, ptr, offset, tp->speculative(), tp->inline_depth());
5245       // else fall through:
5246     case TopPTR:
5247     case AnyNull: {
5248       return make(ptr, _metadata, offset);
5249     }
5250     case BotPTR:
5251     case NotNull:
5252       return TypePtr::make(AnyPtr, ptr, offset, tp->speculative(), tp->inline_depth());
5253     default: typerr(t);
5254     }
5255   }
5256 
5257   case RawPtr:
5258   case KlassPtr:
5259   case OopPtr:
5260   case InstPtr:
5261   case AryPtr:
5262     return TypePtr::BOTTOM;     // Oop meet raw is not well defined
5263 
5264   case MetadataPtr: {
5265     const TypeMetadataPtr *tp = t->is_metadataptr();
5266     Offset offset = meet_offset(tp->offset());
5267     PTR tptr = tp->ptr();
5268     PTR ptr = meet_ptr(tptr);
5269     ciMetadata* md = (tptr == TopPTR) ? metadata() : tp->metadata();
5270     if (tptr == TopPTR || _ptr == TopPTR ||
5271         metadata()->equals(tp->metadata())) {
5272       return make(ptr, md, offset);
5273     }
5274     // metadata is different
5275     if( ptr == Constant ) {  // Cannot be equal constants, so...
5276       if( tptr == Constant && _ptr != Constant)  return t;
5277       if( _ptr == Constant && tptr != Constant)  return this;
5278       ptr = NotNull;            // Fall down in lattice
5279     }
5280     return make(ptr, NULL, offset);
5281     break;
5282   }
5283   } // End of switch
5284   return this;                  // Return the double constant
5285 }
5286 
5287 
5288 //------------------------------xdual------------------------------------------
5289 // Dual of a pure metadata pointer.
5290 const Type *TypeMetadataPtr::xdual() const {
5291   return new TypeMetadataPtr(dual_ptr(), metadata(), dual_offset());
5292 }
5293 
5294 //------------------------------dump2------------------------------------------
5295 #ifndef PRODUCT
5296 void TypeMetadataPtr::dump2( Dict &d, uint depth, outputStream *st ) const {
5297   st->print("metadataptr:%s", ptr_msg[_ptr]);
5298   if( metadata() ) st->print(INTPTR_FORMAT, p2i(metadata()));
5299   switch (offset()) {
5300   case OffsetTop: st->print("+top"); break;
5301   case OffsetBot: st->print("+any"); break;
5302   case         0: break;
5303   default:        st->print("+%d",offset()); break;
5304   }
5305 }
5306 #endif

5339 //------------------------------TypeKlassPtr-----------------------------------
5340 TypeKlassPtr::TypeKlassPtr(PTR ptr, ciKlass* klass, Offset offset, bool flat_array)
5341   : TypePtr(KlassPtr, ptr, offset), _klass(klass), _klass_is_exact(ptr == Constant), _flat_array(flat_array) {
5342    assert(!klass->is_inlinetype() || !klass->flatten_array() || flat_array, "incorrect flatten array bit");
5343    assert(!flat_array || can_be_inline_type(), "incorrect flatten array bit");
5344 }

5346 //------------------------------make-------------------------------------------
5347 // ptr to klass 'k', if Constant, or possibly to a sub-klass if not a Constant
5348 const TypeKlassPtr* TypeKlassPtr::make(PTR ptr, ciKlass* k, Offset offset, bool flat_array) {
5349   assert(k == NULL || k->is_instance_klass() || k->is_array_klass(), "Incorrect type of klass oop");
5350   return (TypeKlassPtr*)(new TypeKlassPtr(ptr, k, offset, flat_array))->hashcons();




5351 }

5353 //------------------------------eq---------------------------------------------
5354 // Structural equality check for Type representations
5355 bool TypeKlassPtr::eq( const Type *t ) const {
5356   const TypeKlassPtr *p = t->is_klassptr();
5357   return klass() == p->klass() && TypePtr::eq(p) && flat_array() == p->flat_array();


5358 }
