5360 //------------------------------hash-------------------------------------------
5361 // Type-specific hashing function.
5362 int TypeKlassPtr::hash(void) const {
5363   return java_add(java_add(klass() != NULL ? klass()->hash() : (jint)0, (jint)TypePtr::hash()), (jint)flat_array());
5364 }
5365 
5366 //------------------------------singleton--------------------------------------
5367 // TRUE if Type is a singleton type, FALSE otherwise.   Singletons are simple
5368 // constants
5369 bool TypeKlassPtr::singleton(void) const {
5370   // detune optimizer to not generate constant klass + constant offset as a constant!
5371   // TopPTR, Null, AnyNull, Constant are all singletons
5372   return (offset() == 0) && !below_centerline(_ptr);
5373 }
5374 
5375 // Do not allow interface-vs.-noninterface joins to collapse to top.
5376 const Type *TypeKlassPtr::filter_helper(const Type *kills, bool include_speculative) const {
5377   // logic here mirrors the one from TypeOopPtr::filter. See comments
5378   // there.
5379   const Type* ft = join_helper(kills, include_speculative);
5380   const TypeKlassPtr* ftkp = ft->isa_klassptr();
5381   const TypeKlassPtr* ktkp = kills->isa_klassptr();
5382 
5383   if (ft->empty()) {
5384     if (!empty() && ktkp != NULL && ktkp->is_loaded() && ktkp->klass()->is_interface())
5385       return kills;             // Uplift to interface
5386 
5387     return Type::TOP;           // Canonical empty value
5388   }
5389 
5390   // Interface klass type could be exact in opposite to interface type,
5391   // return it here instead of incorrect Constant ptr J/L/Object (6894807).
5392   if (ftkp != NULL && ktkp != NULL &&
5393       ftkp->is_loaded() &&  ftkp->klass()->is_interface() &&
5394       !ftkp->klass_is_exact() && // Keep exact interface klass
5395       ktkp->is_loaded() && !ktkp->klass()->is_interface()) {
5396     return ktkp->cast_to_ptr_type(ftkp->ptr());
5397   }
5398 
5399   return ft;
5400 }
5401 
5402 //----------------------compute_klass------------------------------------------
5403 // Compute the defining klass for this class
5404 ciKlass* TypeAryPtr::compute_klass(DEBUG_ONLY(bool verify)) const {
5405   // Compute _klass based on element type.
5406   ciKlass* k_ary = NULL;

5407   const TypeAryPtr *tary;
5408   const Type* el = elem();
5409   if (el->isa_narrowoop()) {
5410     el = el->make_ptr();
5411   }
5412 
5413   // Get element klass
5414   if (el->isa_instptr()) {
5415     // Compute object array klass from element klass
5416     k_ary = ciArrayKlass::make(el->is_oopptr()->klass());
5417   } else if (el->isa_inlinetype()) {
5418     // If element type is TypeInlineType::BOTTOM, inline_klass() will be null.
5419     if (el->inline_klass() != NULL) {
5420       k_ary = ciArrayKlass::make(el->inline_klass());
5421     }
5422   } else if ((tary = el->isa_aryptr()) != NULL) {
5423     // Compute array klass from element klass
5424     ciKlass* k_elem = tary->klass();
5425     // If element type is something like bottom[], k_elem will be null.
5426     if (k_elem != NULL)
5427       k_ary = ciObjArrayKlass::make(k_elem);
5428   } else if ((el->base() == Type::Top) ||
5429              (el->base() == Type::Bottom)) {
5430     // element type of Bottom occurs from meet of basic type
5431     // and object; Top occurs when doing join on Bottom.
5432     // Leave k_ary at NULL.
5433   } else {
5434     // Cannot compute array klass directly from basic type,
5435     // since subtypes of TypeInt all have basic type T_INT.
5436 #ifdef ASSERT
5437     if (verify && el->isa_int()) {
5438       // Check simple cases when verifying klass.
5439       BasicType bt = T_ILLEGAL;
5440       if (el == TypeInt::BYTE) {
5441         bt = T_BYTE;

5466 
5467   // Oops, need to compute _klass and cache it
5468   ciKlass* k_ary = compute_klass();
5469 
5470   if( this != TypeAryPtr::OOPS && this->dual() != TypeAryPtr::OOPS ) {
5471     // The _klass field acts as a cache of the underlying
5472     // ciKlass for this array type.  In order to set the field,
5473     // we need to cast away const-ness.
5474     //
5475     // IMPORTANT NOTE: we *never* set the _klass field for the
5476     // type TypeAryPtr::OOPS.  This Type is shared between all
5477     // active compilations.  However, the ciKlass which represents
5478     // this Type is *not* shared between compilations, so caching
5479     // this value would result in fetching a dangling pointer.
5480     //
5481     // Recomputing the underlying ciKlass for each request is
5482     // a bit less efficient than caching, but calls to
5483     // TypeAryPtr::OOPS->klass() are not common enough to matter.
5484     ((TypeAryPtr*)this)->_klass = k_ary;
5485     if (UseCompressedOops && k_ary != NULL && k_ary->is_obj_array_klass() &&
5486         offset() != 0 && offset() != arrayOopDesc::length_offset_in_bytes()) {
5487       ((TypeAryPtr*)this)->_is_ptr_to_narrowoop = true;
5488     }
5489   }
5490   return k_ary;
5491 }
5492 
5493 
5494 //------------------------------add_offset-------------------------------------
5495 // Access internals of klass object
5496 const TypePtr *TypeKlassPtr::add_offset( intptr_t offset ) const {
5497   return make(_ptr, klass(), xadd_offset(offset), flat_array());
5498 }
5499 
5500 //------------------------------cast_to_ptr_type-------------------------------
5501 const Type *TypeKlassPtr::cast_to_ptr_type(PTR ptr) const {
5502   assert(_base == KlassPtr, "subclass must override cast_to_ptr_type");
5503   if( ptr == _ptr ) return this;
5504   return make(ptr, _klass, _offset, _flat_array);
5505 }

5507 
5508 //-----------------------------cast_to_exactness-------------------------------
5509 const Type *TypeKlassPtr::cast_to_exactness(bool klass_is_exact) const {
5510   if( klass_is_exact == _klass_is_exact ) return this;
5511   return make(klass_is_exact ? Constant : NotNull, _klass, _offset, _flat_array);
5512 }
5513 
5514 
5515 //-----------------------------as_instance_type--------------------------------
5516 // Corresponding type for an instance of the given class.
5517 // It will be NotNull, and exact if and only if the klass type is exact.
5518 const TypeOopPtr* TypeKlassPtr::as_instance_type() const {
5519   ciKlass* k = klass();
5520   assert(k != NULL, "klass should not be NULL");
5521   bool    xk = klass_is_exact();
5522   //return TypeInstPtr::make(TypePtr::NotNull, k, xk, NULL, 0);
5523   const TypeOopPtr* toop = TypeOopPtr::make_from_klass_raw(k);
5524   guarantee(toop != NULL, "need type for given klass");
5525   toop = toop->cast_to_ptr_type(TypePtr::NotNull)->is_oopptr();
5526   if (flat_array() && !klass()->is_inlinetype()) {
5527     toop = toop->is_instptr()->cast_to_flat_array();
5528   }
5529   return toop->cast_to_exactness(xk)->is_oopptr();
5530 }
5531 
5532 
5533 //------------------------------xmeet------------------------------------------
5534 // Compute the MEET of two types, return a new Type object.
5535 const Type    *TypeKlassPtr::xmeet( const Type *t ) const {
5536   // Perform a fast test for common case; meeting the same types together.
5537   if( this == t ) return this;  // Meeting same type-rep?
5538 
5539   // Current "this->_base" is Pointer
5540   switch (t->base()) {          // switch on original type
5541 
5542   case Int:                     // Mixing ints & oops happens when javac
5543   case Long:                    // reuses local variables
5544   case FloatTop:
5545   case FloatCon:
5546   case FloatBot:
5547   case DoubleTop:
5548   case DoubleCon:
5549   case DoubleBot:
5550   case NarrowOop:
5551   case NarrowKlass:
5552   case Bottom:                  // Ye Olde Default
5553     return Type::BOTTOM;
5554   case Top:
5555     return this;
5556 
5557   default:                      // All else is a mistake
5558     typerr(t);
5559 
5560   case AnyPtr: {                // Meeting to AnyPtrs
5561     // Found an AnyPtr type vs self-KlassPtr type
5562     const TypePtr *tp = t->is_ptr();
5563     Offset offset = meet_offset(tp->offset());
5564     PTR ptr = meet_ptr(tp->ptr());
5565     switch (tp->ptr()) {
5566     case TopPTR:
5567       return this;
5568     case Null:
5569       if( ptr == Null ) return TypePtr::make(AnyPtr, ptr, offset, tp->speculative(), tp->inline_depth());
5570     case AnyNull:
5571       return make(ptr, klass(), offset, flat_array());
5572     case BotPTR:
5573     case NotNull:
5574       return TypePtr::make(AnyPtr, ptr, offset, tp->speculative(), tp->inline_depth());
5575     default: typerr(t);
5576     }
5577   }
5578 
5579   case RawPtr:
5580   case MetadataPtr:
5581   case OopPtr:
5582   case AryPtr:                  // Meet with AryPtr
5583   case InstPtr:                 // Meet with InstPtr
5584     return TypePtr::BOTTOM;
5585 
5586   //
5587   //             A-top         }
5588   //           /   |   \       }  Tops
5589   //       B-top A-any C-top   }
5590   //          | /  |  \ |      }  Any-nulls
5591   //       B-any   |   C-any   }
5592   //          |    |    |
5593   //       B-con A-con C-con   } constants; not comparable across classes
5594   //          |    |    |
5595   //       B-not   |   C-not   }
5596   //          | \  |  / |      }  not-nulls
5597   //       B-bot A-not C-bot   }
5598   //           \   |   /       }  Bottoms
5599   //             A-bot         }
5600   //
5601 
5602   case KlassPtr: {  // Meet two KlassPtr types
5603     const TypeKlassPtr *tkls = t->is_klassptr();
5604     Offset  off  = meet_offset(tkls->offset());
5605     PTR  ptr     = meet_ptr(tkls->ptr());
5606 
5607     if (klass() == NULL || tkls->klass() == NULL) {
5608       ciKlass* k = NULL;
5609       if (ptr == Constant) {
5610         k = (klass() == NULL) ? tkls->klass() : klass();
5611       }
5612       return make(ptr, k, off, false);
5613     }
5614 
5615     // Check for easy case; klasses are equal (and perhaps not loaded!)
5616     // If we have constants, then we created oops so classes are loaded
5617     // and we can handle the constants further down.  This case handles
5618     // not-loaded classes
5619     if (ptr != Constant && tkls->klass()->equals(klass()) && flat_array() == tkls->flat_array()) {
5620       return make(ptr, klass(), off, flat_array());
5621     }
5622 
5623     // Classes require inspection in the Java klass hierarchy.  Must be loaded.
5624     ciKlass* tkls_klass = tkls->klass();
5625     ciKlass* this_klass = this->klass();
5626     assert( tkls_klass->is_loaded(), "This class should have been loaded.");
5627     assert( this_klass->is_loaded(), "This class should have been loaded.");
5628     bool tkls_flat_array = tkls->flat_array();
5629     bool this_flat_array  = this->flat_array();
5630     bool flat_array = below_centerline(ptr) ? (this_flat_array && tkls_flat_array) : (this_flat_array || tkls_flat_array);
5631 
5632     // If 'this' type is above the centerline and is a superclass of the
5633     // other, we can treat 'this' as having the same type as the other.
5634     if ((above_centerline(this->ptr())) &&
5635         tkls_klass->is_subtype_of(this_klass)) {
5636       this_klass = tkls_klass;
5637     }
5638     // If 'tinst' type is above the centerline and is a superclass of the
5639     // other, we can treat 'tinst' as having the same type as the other.
5640     if ((above_centerline(tkls->ptr())) &&
5641         this_klass->is_subtype_of(tkls_klass)) {
5642       tkls_klass = this_klass;
5643     }
5644 
5645     // Check for classes now being equal
5646     if (tkls_klass->equals(this_klass)) {
5647       // If the klasses are equal, the constants may still differ.  Fall to
5648       // NotNull if they do (neither constant is NULL; that is a special case
5649       // handled elsewhere).
5650       if( ptr == Constant ) {
5651         if (this->_ptr == Constant && tkls->_ptr == Constant &&
5652             this->klass()->equals(tkls->klass()));
5653         else if (above_centerline(this->ptr()));
5654         else if (above_centerline(tkls->ptr()));
5655         else
5656           ptr = NotNull;
5657       }
5658       return make(ptr, this_klass, off, flat_array);
5659     } // Else classes are not equal
5660 
5661     // Since klasses are different, we require the LCA in the Java
5662     // class hierarchy - which means we have to fall to at least NotNull.
5663     if( ptr == TopPTR || ptr == AnyNull || ptr == Constant )
5664       ptr = NotNull;
5665     // Now we find the LCA of Java classes
5666     ciKlass* k = this_klass->least_common_ancestor(tkls_klass);
5667     return   make(ptr, k, off, k->is_inlinetype() && k->flatten_array());
5668   } // End of case KlassPtr
5669 
5670   } // End of switch
5671   return this;                  // Return the double constant
5672 }
5673 
5674 //------------------------------xdual------------------------------------------
5675 // Dual: compute field-by-field dual
5676 const Type    *TypeKlassPtr::xdual() const {
5677   return new TypeKlassPtr(dual_ptr(), klass(), dual_offset(), flat_array());
5678 }
5679 
5680 //------------------------------get_con----------------------------------------
5681 intptr_t TypeKlassPtr::get_con() const {
5682   assert( _ptr == Null || _ptr == Constant, "" );
5683   assert(offset() >= 0, "");
5684 
5685   if (offset() != 0) {
5686     // After being ported to the compiler interface, the compiler no longer
5687     // directly manipulates the addresses of oops.  Rather, it only has a pointer
5688     // to a handle at compile time.  This handle is embedded in the generated
5689     // code and dereferenced at the time the nmethod is made.  Until that time,
5690     // it is not reasonable to do arithmetic with the addresses of oops (we don't
5691     // have access to the addresses!).  This does not seem to currently happen,
5692     // but this assertion here is to help prevent its occurence.
5693     tty->print_cr("Found oop constant with non-zero offset");
5694     ShouldNotReachHere();
5695   }
5696 
5697   return (intptr_t)klass()->constant_encoding();
5698 }
5699 //------------------------------dump2------------------------------------------
5700 // Dump Klass Type
5701 #ifndef PRODUCT
5702 void TypeKlassPtr::dump2( Dict & d, uint depth, outputStream *st ) const {
5703   switch( _ptr ) {
5704   case Constant:
5705     st->print("precise ");
5706   case NotNull:
5707     {
5708       if (klass() != NULL) {
5709         const char* name = klass()->name()->as_utf8();
5710         st->print("klass %s: " INTPTR_FORMAT, name, p2i(klass()));
5711       } else {
5712         st->print("klass BOTTOM");
5713       }
5714     }
5715   case BotPTR:
5716     if( !WizardMode && !Verbose && !_klass_is_exact ) break;
5717   case TopPTR:
5718   case AnyNull:
5719     st->print(":%s", ptr_msg[_ptr]);
5720     if( _klass_is_exact ) st->print(":exact");
5721     break;
5722   default:
5723     break;
5724   }
5725 
5726   _offset.dump2(st);




5727 
5728   st->print(" *");
5729 }
5730 #endif

5734 //=============================================================================
5735 // Convenience common pre-built types.
5736 
5737 //------------------------------make-------------------------------------------
5738 const TypeFunc *TypeFunc::make(const TypeTuple *domain_sig, const TypeTuple* domain_cc,
5739                                const TypeTuple *range_sig, const TypeTuple *range_cc) {
5740   return (TypeFunc*)(new TypeFunc(domain_sig, domain_cc, range_sig, range_cc))->hashcons();
5741 }
5742 
5743 const TypeFunc *TypeFunc::make(const TypeTuple *domain, const TypeTuple *range) {
5744   return make(domain, domain, range, range);
5745 }
5746 
5747 //------------------------------osr_domain-----------------------------
5748 const TypeTuple* osr_domain() {
5749   const Type **fields = TypeTuple::fields(2);
5750   fields[TypeFunc::Parms+0] = TypeRawPtr::BOTTOM;  // address of osr buffer
5751   return TypeTuple::make(TypeFunc::Parms+1, fields);
5752 }
5753 
5754 //------------------------------make-------------------------------------------
5755 const TypeFunc* TypeFunc::make(ciMethod* method, bool is_osr_compilation) {
5756   Compile* C = Compile::current();
5757   const TypeFunc* tf = NULL;
5758   if (!is_osr_compilation) {
5759     tf = C->last_tf(method); // check cache
5760     if (tf != NULL)  return tf;  // The hit rate here is almost 50%.
5761   }
5762   // Inline types are not passed/returned by reference, instead each field of
5763   // the inline type is passed/returned as an argument. We maintain two views of
5764   // the argument/return list here: one based on the signature (with an inline
5765   // type argument/return as a single slot), one based on the actual calling
5766   // convention (with an inline type argument/return as a list of its fields).
5767   bool has_scalar_args = method->has_scalarized_args() && !is_osr_compilation;
5768   const TypeTuple* domain_sig = is_osr_compilation ? osr_domain() : TypeTuple::make_domain(method, false);
5769   const TypeTuple* domain_cc = has_scalar_args ? TypeTuple::make_domain(method, true) : domain_sig;
5770   ciSignature* sig = method->signature();
5771   bool has_scalar_ret = sig->return_type()->is_inlinetype() && sig->return_type()->as_inline_klass()->can_be_returned_as_fields();
5772   const TypeTuple* range_sig = TypeTuple::make_range(sig, false);
5773   const TypeTuple* range_cc = has_scalar_ret ? TypeTuple::make_range(sig, true) : range_sig;
5774   tf = TypeFunc::make(domain_sig, domain_cc, range_sig, range_cc);
5775   if (!is_osr_compilation) {
5776     C->set_last_tf(method, tf);  // fill cache
5777   }



5778   return tf;
5779 }
5780 
5781 //------------------------------meet-------------------------------------------
5782 // Compute the MEET of two types.  It returns a new Type object.
5783 const Type *TypeFunc::xmeet( const Type *t ) const {
5784   // Perform a fast test for common case; meeting the same types together.
5785   if( this == t ) return this;  // Meeting same type-rep?
5786 
5787   // Current "this->_base" is Func
5788   switch (t->base()) {          // switch on original type
5789 
5790   case Bottom:                  // Ye Olde Default
5791     return t;
5792 
5793   default:                      // All else is a mistake
5794     typerr(t);
5795 
5796   case Top:
5797     break;
5798   }
5799   return this;                  // Return the double constant
5800 }
5801 
5802 //------------------------------xdual------------------------------------------
5803 // Dual: compute field-by-field dual
5804 const Type *TypeFunc::xdual() const {
5805   return this;
5806 }
5807 
5808 //------------------------------eq---------------------------------------------
5809 // Structural equality check for Type representations
5810 bool TypeFunc::eq( const Type *t ) const {
5811   const TypeFunc *a = (const TypeFunc*)t;
5812   return _domain_sig == a->_domain_sig &&
5813     _domain_cc == a->_domain_cc &&
5814     _range_sig == a->_range_sig &&
5815     _range_cc == a->_range_cc;
5816 }
5817 
5818 //------------------------------hash-------------------------------------------
5819 // Type-specific hashing function.
5820 int TypeFunc::hash(void) const {
5821   return (intptr_t)_domain_sig + (intptr_t)_domain_cc + (intptr_t)_range_sig + (intptr_t)_range_cc;
5822 }
5823 
5824 //------------------------------dump2------------------------------------------
5825 // Dump Function Type
5826 #ifndef PRODUCT
5827 void TypeFunc::dump2( Dict &d, uint depth, outputStream *st ) const {
5828   if( _range_sig->cnt() <= Parms )
5829     st->print("void");
5830   else {
5831     uint i;
5832     for (i = Parms; i < _range_sig->cnt()-1; i++) {
5833       _range_sig->field_at(i)->dump2(d,depth,st);
5834       st->print("/");
5835     }
5836     _range_sig->field_at(i)->dump2(d,depth,st);
5837   }
5838   st->print(" ");
5839   st->print("( ");
5840   if( !depth || d[this] ) {     // Check for recursive dump
5841     st->print("...)");
5842     return;
5843   }
5844   d.Insert((void*)this,(void*)this);    // Stop recursion
5845   if (Parms < _domain_sig->cnt())
5846     _domain_sig->field_at(Parms)->dump2(d,depth-1,st);
5847   for (uint i = Parms+1; i < _domain_sig->cnt(); i++) {
5848     st->print(", ");
5849     _domain_sig->field_at(i)->dump2(d,depth-1,st);
5850   }
5851   st->print(" )");
5852 }
5853 #endif
5854 
5855 //------------------------------singleton--------------------------------------
5856 // TRUE if Type is a singleton type, FALSE otherwise.   Singletons are simple
5857 // constants (Ldi nodes).  Singletons are integer, float or double constants
5858 // or a single symbol.
5859 bool TypeFunc::singleton(void) const {
5860   return false;                 // Never a singleton
5861 }
5862 
5863 bool TypeFunc::empty(void) const {
5864   return false;                 // Never empty
5865 }
5866 
5867 
5868 BasicType TypeFunc::return_type() const{
5869   if (range_sig()->cnt() == TypeFunc::Parms) {
5870     return T_VOID;
5871   }
5872   return range_sig()->field_at(TypeFunc::Parms)->basic_type();
5873 }
